To test this, we use sparse autoencoders to decompose polysemantic activations into sparse, monosemantic features and recover candidates for violation-related features.
  We introduce a sensitivity score for identifying features that are preferentially activated on constraint-violated versus well-formed inputs, enabling unsupervised detection of potential violation-specific features. We further propose a conjunctive falsification framework with three criteria evaluated jointly.
  Overall, the results are negative in two respects: (1) the falsification criteria are not jointly satisfied across linguistic phenomena, and (2) no features are consistently shared across all categories. While some phenomena show partial evidence of selective causal structure, the overall pattern provides limited support for a unified set of grammatical violation detectors in current LMs.

### [57] [Latent Causal Void: Explicit Missing-Context Reconstruction for Misinformation Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12156)
*Hui Li,Zhongquan Jian,Jinsong Su,Junfeng Yao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Latent Causal Void（LCV）方法，通过冻结指令调优的大语言模型显式重构每句缺失语境，构建跨源关系异质图进行推理，在双语误信息检测基准上分别超越最强基线2.56和2.84个macro-F1点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动误信息检测方法在处理“遗漏相关信息”的误导性文章时效果不佳。当前感知遗漏的方法要么附加检索到的上下文作为辅助证据，要么推断一个分类性的遗漏信号，但未明确具体缺失的事实。本文旨在显式建模缺失事实本身以提高检测性能。

Method: LCV：1）检索时间对齐的上下文文章；2）利用冻结的指令微调大语言模型为每个句子-文章对生成简短的缺失语境描述；3）将得到的跨源关系文本作为异质图（包含目标句子和上下文文章节点）中的边特征进行图推理。

Result: 在双语（英文和中文）基准上，LCV分别超越最强基线2.56和2.84个macro-F1点。

Conclusion: 显式建模缺失的跨源事实本身，而非仅附加检索证据或预测遗漏信号，是一种有效的遗漏感知误信息检测表示方法。

Abstract: Automatic misinformation detection performs well when deception is visible in what an article explicitly states. However, some misinformation articles remain locally coherent and only become misleading once compared with contemporaneous reports that supply background facts the article omits. We study this omission-relevant setting and observe that current omission-aware approaches typically either attach retrieved context as auxiliary evidence or infer a categorical omission signal, leaving the specific missing fact implicit. We propose \emph{Latent Causal Void} (LCV), a retrieval-guided detector that explicitly reconstructs the missing fact for each target sentence and uses it as a textual cross-source relation in graph reasoning. Concretely, LCV retrieves temporally aligned context articles, asks a frozen instruction-tuned large language model to generate a short missing-context description for each sentence--article pair, and feeds the resulting relation text into a heterograph over target sentences and context articles. On the bilingual benchmark of Sheng et al., LCV improves over the strongest omission-aware baseline by $2.56$ and $2.84$ macro-F1 points on the English and Chinese splits, respectively. The results indicate that modeling the missing cross-source fact itself, rather than only attaching retrieved evidence or predicting an omission signal, is a useful representation for omission-aware misinformation detection.

### [58] [Correcting Selection Bias in Sparse User Feedback for Large Language Model Quality Estimation: A Multi-Agent Hierarchical Bayesian Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12177)
*Andrea Morandi,Mahesh Viswanathan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对LLM生产部署中非随机用户反馈导致的质量评估偏差问题，提出一个三智能体分层贝叶斯pipeline，通过主题聚类、偏置建模和加权合成，在无逐条标注的情况下将偏差控制在4-13个百分点内，且关键依赖反馈通道先验而非质量先验来打破参数退化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生产环境中的LLM收到的用户反馈存在严重的**非随机选择偏差**（反馈集中在满意度分布的极端尾部），直接求均值与真实系统质量相差40-50个百分点，且缺乏逐条交互的真实标注，因此需要一种无监督的偏差校正方法。

Method: 提出三智能体分层贝叶斯pipeline：1）**主题聚类**：UMAP+HDBSCAN对文本嵌入聚类；2）**偏置建模**：两级分层Beta-Binomial模型（NUTS采样），推断每个主题的选择率$s_c$和质量$q_c$，带部分池化；3）**合成**：按真实主题占比$\hatπ_c$加权汇总得到偏差校正后验$\bar Q$及置信区间。关键创新：利用反馈通道的弱先验（正面反馈率与负正比）打破参数退化。

Result: 在UltraFeedback数据集（N=10,232，C=18簇，$Q^\star=0.6249$）上，当偏差比从1:1到30:1变化时，带通道先验的Hierarchical-Informed与真实质量相差4-13个百分点，95%置信区间在50/50随机种子复现中覆盖$Q^\star$（$\kappa_{\max}=10$）。无通道先验的弱先验变体差22-33个百分点。

Conclusion: 生产环境LLM质量评估中的选择偏差可通过主题分层的贝叶斯方法有效校正；关键在于利用反馈通道的弱先验信息（而非质量先验）来打破参数退化，使得无需逐条标注即可获得可信的偏差校正估计。

Abstract: [Abridged] Production LLM deployments receive feedback from a non-random fraction of users: thumbs sit mostly in the tails of the satisfaction distribution, and a naive average over them can land 40-50 percentage points away from true system quality. We treat this as a topic- and sentiment- stratified selection-bias problem and propose a three-agent hierarchical Bayesian pipeline that does not require ground-truth labels on individual interactions. A Topic Clustering Agent partitions the stream via UMAP + HDBSCAN over text embeddings; a Bias Modeling Agent fits a two-stage hierarchical Beta-Binomial under NUTS, inferring per-topic selection rates $s_c$ and quality $q_c$ with partial pooling; a Synthesis Agent reweights $q_c$ by true topic prevalence $\hatπ_c = n_c/N$ to report a bias-corrected aggregate posterior $\bar Q = \sum_c \hatπ_c q_c$ with credible interval, plus drift signals for online recalibration. Validation uses UltraFeedback (N=10,232 retained interactions, $C=18$ clusters, $Q^\star=0.6249$) with simulated topic- and sentiment-dependent selection biases. We compare five Bayesian variants against Naive and IPW baselines. A mild prior on the feedback channel (typical positive-feedback rate and negative-to-positive ratio, both readable from any production dashboard without labels) keeps Hierarchical-Informed within 4-13 pp of $Q^\star$ as the bias ratio sweeps from 1:1 to 30:1, with 95% credible intervals covering $Q^\star$ in 50/50 random-seed replicates at $κ_{\max}=10$. Without channel-side priors, every weak-prior variant misses $Q^\star$ by 22-33 pp: the per-cluster sufficient statistics admit a one-parameter family of equally good fits, and the prior on the bias channel (not on latent quality) is what breaks the degeneracy.

### [59] [Mitigating Context-Memory Conflicts in LLMs through Dynamic Cognitive Reconciliation Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12185)
*Yigeng Zhou,Wu Li,Yifan Lu,Yequan Wang,Xuebo Liu,Wenya Wang,Jun Yu,Min Zhang,Jing Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出动态认知调和解码（DCRD），一种两阶段解码方法，通过分析注意力图预测上下文-记忆冲突，并动态选择贪婪解码或基于上下文忠实度的解码路径。在四个LLM、六个QA数据集上达到SOTA，并构建了知识冲突基准ConflictKG。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在预训练中积累了大量参数化知识，但当上下文中的外部知识与过时/错误的参数化知识冲突时，会产生知识冲突问题。现有对比解码方法在无冲突场景下会破坏输出分布，动态方法虽试图衡量冲突程度但仍难以应对复杂现实情况。

Method: 提出两阶段解码方法DCRD：第一阶段分析注意力图，评估上下文忠实度并预测潜在冲突；第二阶段根据预测结果将输入导向两条解码路径之一——（1）贪心解码，或（2）基于上下文忠实度的动态解码。同时构建了ConflictKG知识冲突QA基准。

Conclusion: DCRD能够高效处理知识冲突，同时在无冲突场景下保持高准确率和解码效率，验证了其有效性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Large language models accumulate extensive parametric knowledge through pre-training. However, knowledge conflicts occur when outdated or incorrect parametric knowledge conflicts with external knowledge in the context. Existing methods address knowledge conflicts through contrastive decoding, but in conflict-free scenarios, static approaches disrupt output distribution. Other dynamic decoding methods attempt to measure the degree of conflict but still struggle with complex real-world situations. In this paper, we propose a two-stage decoding method called Dynamic Cognitive Reconciliation Decoding (DCRD), to predict and mitigate context-memory conflicts. DCRD first analyzes the attention map to assess context fidelity and predict potential conflicts. Based on this prediction, the input is directed to one of two decoding paths: (1) greedy decoding, or (2) context fidelity-based dynamic decoding. This design enables DCRD to handle conflicts efficiently while maintaining high accuracy and decoding efficiency in conflict-free cases. Additionally, to simulate scenarios with frequent knowledge updates, we constructed ConflictKG, a knowledge conflict QA benchmark. Experiments on four LLMs across six QA datasets show that DCRD outperforms all baselines, achieving state-of-the-art performance.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将稀疏自编码器（SAE）应用于Whisper（基于Transformer的ASR模型），在Whisper编码器提取的帧级嵌入上训练一个高维稀疏潜在空间，以投影和解释稠密表示。

Abstract: Understanding the internal machinations of deep Transformer-based NLP models is more crucial than ever as these models see widespread use in various domains that affect the public at large, such as industry, academia, finance, health. While these models have advanced rapidly, their internal mechanisms remain largely a mystery. Techniques such as Sparse Autoencoders (SAE) have emerged to understand these mechanisms by projecting dense representations into a sparse vector. While existing research has demonstrated the viability of the SAE in interpreting text-based Large Language Models (LLMs), there are no equivalent studies that demonstrate the application of a SAE to audio processing models like Automatic Speech Recognizers (ASRs). In this work, a SAE is applied to Whisper, a Transformer-based ASR, training a high-dimensional sparse latent space on frame-level embeddings extracted from the Whisper encoder. Our work uncovers diverse monosemantic features across linguistic and non-linguistic boundaries, and demonstrates cross-lingual feature steering. This work establishes the viability of a SAE model and demonstrates that Whisper encodes a rich amount of linguistic information.

### [61] [Combining On-Policy Optimization and Distillation for Long-Context Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12227)
*Miguel Moura Ramos,Duarte M. Alves,André F. T. Martins*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出dGRPO方法，结合策略优化（GRPO）与知识蒸馏（OPD）来解决长上下文推理中的对齐问题，并引入合成数据集LongBlocks，实验表明该方法比单独使用SFT、KD或GRPO更稳定有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在面对长上下文任务时各有局限：SFT/KD存在曝光偏差和误差累积；GRPO奖励稀疏、训练不稳定；OPD虽提供密集指导但无法直接优化任意奖励信号。因此需要一种能结合两者优势的方法。

Method: 提出dGRPO，在GRPO基础上引入来自更强教师模型的密集逐token指导（通过OPD），形成统一的训练目标。同时构建了LongBlocks合成数据集，包含多跳推理、上下文 grounding 和长文本生成等任务。

Result: 实验表明dGRPO在长上下文推理任务上优于离线训练、稀疏奖励GRPO等基线方法，训练更稳定、样本效率更高，且不损失短上下文能力。

Conclusion: 将基于结果的策略优化与知识蒸馏结合在单一目标中，为长上下文对齐提供了一条更稳定有效的路径。

Abstract: Adapting large language models (LLMs) to long-context tasks requires post-training methods that remain accurate and coherent over thousands of tokens. Existing approaches are limited in several ways: 1) off-policy methods such as supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and knowledge distillation (KD) suffer from exposure bias and limited recovery from model-generated errors over long horizons; 2) on-policy reinforcement learning methods such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) better align training with model-generated states, but are unstable and sample-inefficient due to sparse rewards; 3) on-policy distillation (OPD) provides dense token-level guidance, but does not directly optimize arbitrary reward signals. In this paper, we propose Distilled Group Relative Policy Optimization (dGRPO), a method for long-context reasoning that augments GRPO with dense guidance from a stronger teacher via OPD. We also introduce LongBlocks, a synthetic long-context dataset spanning multi-hop reasoning, contextual grounding, and long-form generation. We conduct extensive experiments and ablations comparing off-policy training, sparse-reward GRPO, and our combined approach, leading to an improved recipe for long-context alignment. Overall, our results show that combining outcome-based policy optimization with knowledge distillation in a single objective provides a more stable and effective path to long-context reasoning, while preserving short-context capabilities.

### [62] [Mind the Pause: Disfluency-Aware Objective Tuning for Multilingual Speech Correction with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12242)
*Deepak Kumar,Baban Gain,Asif Ekbal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出一个多语言ASR不流利纠正流程：先用序列标注器标记不流利token，再通过指令微调LLM重写为流畅文本，并加入对比学习目标以惩罚保留不流利token。在印地语、孟加拉语、马拉地语上取得一致改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ASR转录中的不流利（如填充词、重复、错误开头）会降低可读性并影响下游系统。现有方法主要基于经典模型检测并删除不流利token，但常破坏语法结构和语义连贯性；而LLM相关工作多聚焦于检测或数据增强，缺乏全面的纠正方案。

Method: 提出多语言纠正流程：(1) 序列标注器标记不流利token；(2) 以这些信号指导LLM进行指令微调，重写为流畅文本；(3) 增加对比学习目标，惩罚模型再现不流利token，保持语法和语义。

Result: 在印地语、孟加拉语、马拉地语三种印度语言上，相比包括多语言序列到序列模型在内的强基线，该方法获得一致性提升。

Abstract: Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) transcripts often contain disfluencies, such as fillers, repetitions, and false starts, which reduce readability and hinder downstream applications like chatbots and voice assistants. If left unaddressed, such disfluencies can significantly degrade the reliability of downstream systems. Most existing approaches rely on classical models that focus on identifying disfluent tokens for removal. While this strategy is effective to some extent, it often disrupts grammatical structure and semantic coherence, leading to incomplete or unnatural sentences. Recent literature explored the use of large language models (LLMs); however, these efforts have primarily focused on disfluency detection or data augmentation, rather than performing comprehensive correction. We propose a multilingual correction pipeline where a sequence tagger first marks disfluent tokens, and these signals guide instruction fine-tuning of an LLM to rewrite transcripts into fluent text. To further improve reliability, we add a contrastive learning objective that penalizes the reproduction of disfluent tokens, encouraging the model to preserve grammar and meaning while removing disfluent artifacts. Our experiments across three Indian languages, namely Hindi, Bengali, and Marathi show consistent improvements over strong baselines, including multilingual sequence-to-sequence models. These results highlight that detection-only strategies are insufficient. Combining token-level cues with instruction tuning and contrastive learning provides a practical and scalable solution for multilingual disfluency correction in speech-driven NLP systems. We make the codes publicly available at https://github.com/deepak-kumar-98/Mind-the-Pause.

### [63] [PreScam: A Benchmark for Predicting Scam Progression from Early Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12243)
*Weixiang Sun,Shang Ma,Yiyang Li,Tianyi Ma,Zehong Wang,Colby Nelson,Xusheng Xiao,Yanfang Ye*

Main category: cs.CL

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从用户提交的诈骗举报中筛选并结构化177,989条原始报告，最终构建11,573个对话式诈骗实例，涵盖20个诈骗类别。每个实例按照提出的诈骗杀伤链（scam kill chain）进行层次化结构标注，并在对话轮次级别标注诈骗者的心理操作和受害者的回应。设计了两个评估任务：实时终止预测（判断对话是否接近终止阶段）和诈骗者行为预测（预测诈骗者下一步行动）。

Result: 监督编码器在实时终止预测任务上大幅优于零样本大语言模型；即使对于强大语言模型，下一步行为预测也仅取得中等成功。模型能够捕捉部分诈骗相关线索，但在跨轮次追踪风险升级和操纵展开方面仍存在困难。

Conclusion: 当前模型在表面流畅性和进展建模之间存在明显差距，尚难以真正理解对话式诈骗的动态演化过程，亟需更深入的进展感知建模方法。

Abstract: Conversational scams, such as romance and investment scams, are emerging as a major form of online fraud. Unlike one-shot scam lures such as fake lottery or unpaid toll messages, they unfold through multi-turn conversations in which scammers gradually manipulate victims using evolving psychological techniques. However, existing research mainly focuses on static scam detection or synthetic scams, leaving open whether language models can understand how real-world scams progress over time. We introduce PreScam, a benchmark for modeling scam progression from early conversations. Built from user-submitted scam reports, PreScam filters and structures 177,989 raw reports into 11,573 conversational scam instances spanning 20 scam categories. Each instance is hierarchically structured according to the scam lifecycle defined by the proposed scam kill chain, and further annotated at the turn level with scammer psychological actions and victim responses. We benchmark models on two tasks: real-time termination prediction, which estimates whether a conversation is approaching the termination stage, and scammer action prediction, which forecasts the scammer's subsequent actions. Results show a clear gap between surface-level fluency and progression modeling: supervised encoders substantially outperform zero-shot LLMs on real-time termination prediction, while next-action prediction remains only moderately successful even for strong LLMs. Taken together, these results show that current models can capture some scam-related cues, yet still struggle to track how risk escalates and how manipulation unfolds across turns.

### [64] [PRISM: Pareto-Efficient Retrieval over Intent-Aware Structured Memory for Long-Horizon Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12260)
*Jingyi Peng,Zhongwei Wan,Weiting Liu,Qiuzhuang Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PRISM是一个免训练的检索端框架，通过将长期记忆视为图结构上的联合检索与压缩问题，在极小上下文预算下实现了比所有基线更高的准确性，占据了过去空白的高精度-低成本前沿区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么无限扩展上下文窗口而不优化检索内容，要么在摄入阶段做繁重的事实抽取导致高token成本，要么依赖启发式图遍历导致准确率和效率双双不佳。缺乏一种在不增加训练开销和上下文预算的前提下高效检索并压缩证据的方法。

Method: PRISM包含四个正交的推理时组件：1) 层次化束搜索（在类型化关系路径上搜索）；2) 查询敏感边成本计算（对齐查询意图）；3) 证据压缩（将候选束压缩为紧凑的答案上下文）；4) 自适应意图路由（大多数查询走零LLM层级）。将检索建模为类型化路径模板上的最小成本选择问题，配合LLM端压缩步骤。

Result: 在LoCoMo基准上，PRISM在远小于基线的上下文预算下取得了更高的LLM-judge准确率，占据精度-成本前沿中此前空白的区域，实现了答案质量与检索效率之间的优越平衡。

Conclusion: PRISM通过将长期记忆管理重新定义为联合检索与压缩问题，在不微调和不修改上游摄入流水线的前提下，在严格上下文预算下准确呈现证据，实现了极佳的准确率与成本平衡。

Abstract: Long-horizon language agents accumulate conversation history far faster than any fixed context window can hold, making memory management critical to both answer accuracy and serving cost. Existing approaches either expand the context window without addressing what is retrieved, perform heavy ingestion-time fact extraction at substantial token cost, or rely on heuristic graph traversal that leaves both accuracy and efficiency on the table. We present PRISM, a training-free retrieval-side framework that treats long-horizon memory as a joint retrieval-and-compression problem over a graph-structured memory. PRISM combines four orthogonal inference-time components: Hierarchical Bundle Search over typed relation paths, Query-Sensitive Edge Costing that aligns traversal with detected query intent, Evidence Compression that compresses the candidate bundle into a compact answer-side context, and Adaptive Intent Routing that routes most queries through zero-LLM tiers. By formulating retrieval as min-cost selection over typed path templates and pairing it with an LLM-side compression step, PRISM surfaces the right evidence under a strict context budget without any fine-tuning or modification to the upstream ingestion pipeline. Experiments on the LoCoMo benchmark show that PRISM delivers substantially higher LLM-judge accuracy than every same-protocol baseline at an order-of-magnitude smaller context budget, occupying a previously empty corner of the accuracy-context-cost frontier and demonstrating a superior balance between answer quality and retrieval efficiency.

</details>


### [65] [What makes a word hard to learn? Modeling L1 influence on English vocabulary difficulty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12281)
*Jonas Mayer Martins,Zhuojing Huang,Aaricia Herygers,Lisa Beinborn*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用梯度提升模型（gradient-boosted models），训练基于词汇熟悉度（如词频）、意义、表面形式和跨语言迁移等特征，并通过Shapley值确定各特征组的重要性。

Result: 词汇熟悉度是所有三种母语（西班牙语、德语、中文）学习者共有的主导特征组；西班牙语和德语学习者额外依赖正字法迁移，而中文学习者则缺乏这种迁移机制，其难度由熟悉度和表面特征共同决定。

Abstract: What makes a word difficult to learn, and how does the difficulty depend on the learner's native language? Using Shapley values, we determine the importance of each feature group. Word familiarity is the dominant feature group shared by all three languages. However, predictions for Spanish- and German-speaking learners rely additionally on orthographic transfer. This transfer mechanism is unavailable to Chinese learners, whose difficulty is shaped by a combination of familiarity and surface features alone. Our models provide interpretable, L1-tailored difficulty estimates that can be used to design vocabulary curricula.

*Truong Nguyen,Tien-Phat Nguyen,Linh Ngo Van,Duy Minh Ho Nguyen,Khoa Doan,Trung Le*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Token-level Bregman Preference Optimization (TBPO)，一种基于token级Bradley-Terry偏好模型的直接偏好优化方法，通过Bregman散度密度比匹配目标，在保持DPO简洁性的同时实现token级最优策略，在多个基准上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DPO方法在序列级别建模偏好，但文本生成本质上是逐token决策过程，导致每个前缀（状态）的最优性被隐式处理，缺乏显式的token级偏好优化框架。

Method: 提出两阶段方法：（1）TBPO-Q：显式学习轻量级状态基线；（2）TBPO-A：通过优势归一化移除基线。核心是使用Bregman散度进行密度比匹配，泛化逻辑损失/DPO损失。

Result: 在指令遵循、有用性/无害性、摘要生成等基准上，TBPO在对齐质量、训练稳定性和输出多样性方面均优于序列级和token级基线方法。

Conclusion: TBPO成功将DPO扩展到token级偏好优化，既保留了DPO的简洁性，又通过显式的token级建模提升了对齐效果，证明了在偏好优化中考虑per-token最优性的重要性。

Abstract: Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) is a widely used RL-free method for aligning language models from pairwise preferences, but it models preferences over full sequences even though generation is driven by per-token decisions. Existing token-level extensions typically decompose a sequence-level Bradley-Terry objective across timesteps, leaving per-prefix (state-wise) optimality implicit. We study how to recover token-level preference optimality using only standard sequence-level pairwise comparisons. We introduce Token-level Bregman Preference Optimization (TBPO), which posits a token-level Bradley-Terry preference model over next-token actions conditioned on the prefix, and derive a Bregman-divergence density-ratio matching objective that generalizes the logistic/DPO loss while preserving the optimal policy induced by the token-level model and maintaining DPO-like simplicity. We introduce two instantiations: TBPO-Q, which explicitly learns a lightweight state baseline, and TBPO-A, which removes the baseline through advantage normalization. Across instruction following, helpfulness/harmlessness, and summarization benchmarks, TBPO improves alignment quality and training stability and increases output diversity relative to strong sequence-level and token-level baselines.

### [67] [GKnow: Measuring the Entanglement of Gender Bias and Factual Gender](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12299)
*Leonor Veloso,Hinrich Schütze*

TL;DR: 本文通过构建GKnow基准，研究了语言模型中性别偏见与事实性别知识的纠缠关系，发现两者在神经元和电路层面严重纠缠，使得神经元消融作为去偏见方法不可靠，且现有偏见基准可能掩盖事实性别知识的损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对神经网络中性别相关预测的机制解读存在两个问题：(i) 过于聚焦特定性别任务（如代词预测）；(ii) 未能区分事实性别输出（基于语义属性的正确性别假设）与性别偏见输出（基于刻板印象）。

Method: 1. 构建GKnow基准，评估语言模型在不同类型性别预测中的性别知识与性别偏见。2. 通过电路和单个神经元分析，识别负责性别预测的组件。3. 在DiFair、GKnow测试集和StereoSet上进行神经元消融实验。

Conclusion: 性别偏见与事实性别知识在神经层面高度纠缠，简单消融无法有效去除偏见而同时保持事实知识，GKnow基准有助于推动更鲁棒的性别偏见评估方法的发展。

Abstract: Recent works have analyzed the impact of individual components of neural networks on gendered predictions, often with a focus on mitigating gender bias. However, mechanistic interpretations of gender tend to (i) focus on a very specific gender-related task, such as gendered pronoun prediction, or (ii) fail to distinguish between the production of factually gendered outputs (the correct assumption of gender given a word that carries gender as a semantic property) and gender biased outputs (based on a stereotype). To address these issues, we curate \gknow, a benchmark to assess gender knowledge and gender bias in language models across different types of gender-related predictions. \gknow allows us to identify and analyze circuits and individual neurons responsible for gendered predictions. We test the impact of neuron ablation on benchmarks for disentangling stereotypical and factual gender (DiFair and the test set of GKnow), as well as StereoSet. Results show that gender bias and factual gender are severely entangled on the level of both circuits and neurons, entailing that ablation is an unreliable debiasing method. Furthermore, we show that benchmarks for evaluating gender bias can hide the decrease in factual gender knowledge that accompanies neuron ablation. We curate GKnow as a contribution to the continuous development of robust gender bias benchmarks.

Abstract: Multi-hop question answering (QA) remains a significant challenge in the biomedical domain, requiring systems to integrate information across multiple sources to answer complex questions.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中小企业的数据录入系统对分类错误高度脆弱，尤其是当名义类别存在语义或形态相似性时，人机交互产生的错误事后不可恢复，且现有标准化工具孤立评估语义和形态维度、过度依赖标准词典，对富含自定义SKU、缩写和专业术语的中小企业主数据无效。

Method: ISEC整合三个维度：①通过词嵌入计算语义距离；②通过改进的Damerau-Levenshtein算法计算自定义加权形态变换成本；③引入经验频率。利用向量数据库架构将计算复杂度降低约195倍，输出类别对的序数复合评分以排序其结构混淆敏感性。

Result: 在政府司法记录、零售库存和合成ISO编码金属加工目录三个异构数据集上验证有效性，性能较暴力方法提升约195倍，能主动检测嵌入在类别数据资产中的潜在结构风险。

Conclusion: ISEC是一种可扩展的主动式数据治理工具，能够帮助中小企业在数据输入前识别类别间的结构混淆风险，从而防止错误传播至关键绩效指标并误导管理决策。

Abstract: Data entry systems remain structurally vulnerable to categorical misclassifications, particularly in small and medium sized enterprises (SMEs). When nominal categories exhibit semantic or morphological proximity, human machine interaction may produce errors that are irrecoverable ex post. In the absence of automated input controls, manual data entry frequently generates irrecoverable categorical distortions that propagate into Key Performance Indicators (KPIs), thereby misleading managerial decision making. State of the art normalization tools typically evaluate semantic and morphological dimensions in isolation and rely heavily on standard dictionaries, rendering them ineffective for SME master data rich in custom SKUs, abbreviations, and domain-specific technical jargon. This paper introduces the Categorical Error Sensitivity Index (ISEC), an ordinal composite score designed to rank category pairs according to their structural susceptibility to confusion. ISEC integrates semantic distance (via word embeddings), custom weighted morphological transformation costs (through an adapted Damerau Levenshtein algorithm), and empirical frequency into a unified, mathematically robust preventive framework. By leveraging vector database architectures, ISEC reduces computational complexity, achieving approximately a 195x performance improvement over brute-force methods. Validated across three heterogeneous datasets: governmental judicial records, retail inventory, and a synthetic ISO coded metalworking catalog, ISEC provides a scalable and proactive data governance instrument that enables SMEs to detect latent structural risk embedded within their categorical data assets.

</details>

*Michela Lorandi,Anya Belz*

Method: 探索三种策略：(1)多任务联合训练；(2)推理时组合独立训练的PEFT权重矩阵；(3)推理时组合独立训练的PEFT模块输出。使用QLoRA作为PEFT方法，在情感控制、主题控制、多属性控制三个可控文本生成数据集上测试三个不同的LLM。

Abstract: Parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) techniques offer task-specific fine-tuning at a fraction of the cost of full fine-tuning, but require separate fine-tuning for every new task (combination). We test these approaches on three different LLMs, QLoRA as the PEFT technique, and three sets of controlled text generation datasets for sentiment control, topic control, and multi-attribute control. We find that summing PEFT module outputs is a particularly strong composition method, which consistently either outperforms or matches the performance of alternative approaches. This is the case even when comparing against single-task specialised modules on the single-task test set, where three-module output composition achieves an average 2% point performance increase across all models for sentiment control.

Existing biomedical question answering (QA) benchmarks are limited in this respect. Multiple-choice formats can allow models to succeed through answer elimination rather than inference, while widely circulated exam-style datasets are increasingly vulnerable to performance saturation and training data contamination. MedHopQA is a disease-centered multi-hop reasoning benchmark consisting of 1,000 expert-curated question-answer pairs introduced as a shared task at BioCreative IX. To reduce leaderboard gaming and contamination risk, the 1,000 scored questions are embedded within a publicly downloadable set of 10,000 questions, with answers withheld, on a CodaBench leaderboard. MedHopQA provides both a benchmark and a reusable framework for constructing future biomedical QA datasets that prioritize compositional reasoning, saturation resistance, and contamination resistance as core design constraints.

### [73] [Pretraining Exposure Explains Popularity Judgments in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12382)
*Jamshid Mozafari,Bhawna Piryani,Adam Jatowt*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文首次基于完全可观测的预训练数据（OLMo + Dolma，7.4万亿token），直接分析了2000个实体的曝光统计与LLM流行度偏好的关系。研究发现：预训练曝光与Wikipedia流行度高度相关，但LLM的流行度判断更接近预训练曝光而非Wikipedia，且这一效应在大模型和长尾分布中更强。结论证实：流行度偏好的根源在于预训练数据统计，而非外部流行度信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往关于LLM流行度偏好的研究无法区分"反映真实世界流行度"与"反映预训练统计偏差"，因为大多数训练语料不可见。本文利用完全开源的OLMo模型和Dolma语料库，首次实现从预训练数据角度直接量化并解释流行度偏好的成因。

Method: 1）使用OLMo模型和Dolma语料库（7.4万亿token），计算2000个实体（分5类：人物、地点、组织、艺术品、产品）在预训练中的精确曝光统计；2）对比预训练曝光度、Wikipedia页面浏览量、以及两种LLM流行度信号（直接标量估计和两两比较）之间的关系；3）分析模型规模、实体类型和长尾分布对结果的影响。

Result: 1）预训练曝光与Wikipedia流行度强相关，说明曝光是训练期间真实世界显著性的有效代理；2）LLM的流行度判断与预训练曝光的对齐程度高于与Wikipedia的对齐程度，尤其在两两比较方式下更明显；3）大模型的对齐更强；4）在长尾区域（Wikipedia流行度不可靠时），LLM的判断仍与预训练曝光保持一致。

Conclusion: LLM的流行度先验主要由预训练统计塑造，而非真实世界的外部流行度信号。这提供了直接的实证证据：数据曝光在驱动流行度偏见中起到核心作用。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) exhibit systematic preferences for well-known entities, a phenomenon often attributed to popularity bias. However, the extent to which these preferences reflect real-world popularity versus statistical exposure during pretraining remains unclear, largely due to the inaccessibility of most training corpora. We provide the first direct, large-scale analysis of popularity bias grounded in fully observable pretraining data. Leveraging the open OLMo models and their complete pretraining corpus, Dolma, we compute precise entity-level exposure statistics across 7.4 trillion tokens. We analyze 2,000 entities spanning five types (Person, Location, Organization, Art, Product) and compare pretraining exposure against Wikipedia pageviews and two elicited LLM popularity signals: direct scalar estimation and pairwise comparison. Our results show that pretraining exposure strongly correlates with Wikipedia popularity, validating exposure as a meaningful proxy for real-world salience during the training period. More importantly, we find that LLM popularity judgments align more closely with exposure than with Wikipedia, especially when elicited via pairwise comparisons. This alignment is strongest for larger models and persists in the long tail, where Wikipedia popularity becomes unreliable. Overall, our findings demonstrate that popularity priors in LLMs are primarily shaped by pretraining statistics rather than external popularity signals, offering concrete evidence that data exposure plays a central role in driving popularity bias.

### [77] [Stories in Space: In-Context Learning Trajectories in Conceptual Belief Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12412)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明LLM的上下文学习可视为贝叶斯推理，但潜在假设空间的结构尚不清楚。本文旨在揭示这一假设空间的几何结构。

Method: 以故事理解作为自然动态信念更新的场景，结合行为分析（模型输出）和表征分析（内部表示），利用低维流形建模信念轨迹，并通过线性探测和解码预测行为，最后进行表征干预的因果实验。

Result: (1)信念更新可被低维结构化流形上的轨迹良好描述；(2)该结构在行为与内部表征中一致反映，可用线性探针解码预测行为；(3)对表征的干预能因果性地引导信念轨迹，其效果可由概念空间的几何结构预测。

Conclusion: 为LLM中信念动态提供了几何解释，将上下文学习的贝叶斯解释建立在结构化概念表征之上，揭示了LLM推理背后潜在的几何框架。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) update their behavior in context, which can be viewed as a form of Bayesian inference. However, the structure of the latent hypothesis space over which this inference operates remains unclear. In this work, we propose that LLMs assign beliefs over a low-dimensional geometric space - a conceptual belief space - and that in-context learning corresponds to a trajectory through this space as beliefs are updated over time. Using story understanding as a natural setting for dynamic belief updating, we combine behavioral and representational analyses to study these trajectories. We find that (1) belief updates are well-described as trajectories on low-dimensional, structured manifolds; (2) this structure is reflected consistently in both model behavior and internal representations and can be decoded with simple linear probes to predict behavior; and (3) interventions on these representations causally steer belief trajectories, with effects that can be predicted from the geometry of the conceptual space. Together, our results provide a geometric account of belief dynamics in LLMs, grounding Bayesian interpretations of in-context learning in structured conceptual representations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在特定任务微调（如GenRetrieval）时，会迅速发生灾难性遗忘，导致其通用的语言推理能力退化。作者发现遗忘速度与微调后模型参数和原始参数之间的距离相关。

Method: 提出ORBIT方法，主动追踪微调模型与初始模型权重之间的距离，当该距离超过最大阈值时，采用权重平均策略来约束模型在GenRetrieval微调过程中的参数漂移。

Result: ORBIT在文本生成和检索性能上均优于常见的持续学习基线和相关的正则化方法（包括同样使用权重平均的方法），有效保留了模型的通用能力。

Conclusion: 通过动态监控参数距离并进行权重平均约束，可以有效缓解微调过程中的灾难性遗忘问题，为生成式检索任务提供了一种高效的持续学习方案。

Abstract: Despite the rapid advancements in large language model (LLM) development, fine-tuning them for specific tasks often results in the catastrophic forgetting of their general, language-based reasoning abilities. This work investigates and addresses this challenge in the context of the Generative Retrieval (GenRetrieval) task. During GenRetrieval fine-tuning, we find this forgetting occurs rapidly and correlates with the distance between the fine-tuned and original model parameters. Given these observations, we propose ORBIT, a novel approach that actively tracks the distance between fine-tuned and initial model weights, and uses a weight averaging strategy to constrain model drift during GenRetrieval fine-tuning when this inter-model distance exceeds a maximum threshold. Our results show that ORBIT retains substantial text and retrieval performance by outperforming both common continual learning baselines and related regularization methods that also employ weight averaging.

</details>


### [79] [Geometric Factual Recall in Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12426)
*Shauli Ravfogel,Gilad Yehudai,Joan Bruna,Alberto Bietti*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出并证明了一种新的几何式记忆机制：Transformer语言模型可以通过对数维度的嵌入空间以线性叠加方式存储事实关联，MLP层并非传统的键值记忆，而是充当关系条件化的选择器。这一机制在单层单跳和多跳场景下均有理论保证和实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战传统观点：内部权重矩阵作为键值对记忆需要参数量与事实数量线性增长。本文旨在揭示Transformer记忆事实关联的另一种几何形式机制，并解释MLP层的真实作用。

Method: 在控制实验中，单层Transformer需要记忆从主语到共享属性集的随机双射。理论上证明对数维度的嵌入维度足以支持这种记忆——主语嵌入编码其关联属性向量的线性叠加，小MLP通过ReLU门控作为关系条件化选择器。扩展到多跳场景（链式关系查询），给出有/无思维链的构造，并匹配信息论下界。实验验证梯度下降发现预期结构，且MLP在零样本条件下可迁移到全新双射。

Result: 理论证明对数嵌入维度即可实现事实记忆；实验证实模型确实学到这种几何式结构；MLP学到的是通用的选择机制而非特定事实，在主语嵌入重新初始化后可零样本迁移到全新双射。

Conclusion: Transformer语言模型的记忆机制存在一种几何形式：嵌入空间以线性叠加编码关系结构，MLP扮演关系条件化选择器而非键值记忆。这提供了对模型记忆容量与泛化能力的新理解，并揭示了深度与表达能力之间的可证明权衡。

Abstract: How do transformer language models memorize factual associations? A common view casts internal weight matrices as associative memories over pairs of embeddings, requiring parameter counts that scale linearly with the number of facts. We develop a theoretical and empirical account of an alternative, \emph{geometric} form of memorization in which learned embeddings encode relational structure directly, and the MLP plays a qualitatively different role. In a controlled setting where a single-layer transformer must memorize random bijections from subjects to a shared attribute set, we prove that a logarithmic embedding dimension suffices: subject embeddings encode \emph{linear superpositions} of their associated attribute vectors, and a small MLP acts as a relation-conditioned selector that extracts the relevant attribute via ReLU gating, and not as an associative key-value mapping. We extend these results to the multi-hop setting -- chains of relational queries such as ``Who is the mother of the wife of $x$?'' -- providing constructions with and without chain-of-thought that exhibit a provable capacity-depth tradeoff, complemented by a matching information-theoretic lower bound. Empirically, gradient descent discovers solutions with precisely the predicted structure. Once trained, the MLP transfers zero-shot to entirely new bijections when subject embeddings are appropriately re-initialized, revealing that it has learned a generic selection mechanism rather than memorized any particular set of facts.

</details>


### [80] [A Causal Language Modeling Detour Improves Encoder Continued Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12438)
*Rian Touchent,Eric de la Clergerie*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 在领域适应中，先用因果语言模型（CLM）训练再过渡到掩码语言模型（MLM），相比纯MLM训练能获得更好的下游任务表现。该方法的优势源于CLM对低层Transformer层的密集监督，且这种表征变化在后续MLM阶段得以保持，并随模型容量增大而增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在领域适应编码器时，用CLM替代传统MLM能否提升下游性能，并解释其背后的原因。

Method: 先进行CLM训练（临时切换），再短时间进行MLM衰减（decay），与从头到尾纯MLM训练对比。通过冻结不同层的实验分析各层贡献，研究表征变化在MLM阶段是否持续。

Result: 在生物医学文本上用ModernBERT，CLM detour在8个法语和11个英语生物医学任务上分别比MLM基线高出+1.2-2.8pp和+0.3-0.8pp。CLM的密集监督主要影响低层（0-7层），冻结低层会消除收益，冻结中层则保持收益。

Conclusion: CLM detour是一种有效的领域适应策略，收益来源于CLM对低层的密集监督，且表征变化在后续MLM阶段得以保留，随模型容量提升而增强。发布了ModernCamemBERT-bio和ModernBERT-bio作为SOTA生物医学编码器。

Abstract: When adapting an encoder to a new domain, the standard approach is to continue training with Masked Language Modeling (MLM). We show that temporarily switching to Causal Language Modeling (CLM) followed by a short MLM decay improves downstream performance. On biomedical texts with ModernBERT, this CLM detour outperforms MLM baselines trained on identical data and compute across 8 French and 11 English biomedical tasks, by +1.2-2.8pp and +0.3-0.8pp respectively, depending on model size. We investigate the reasons for these gains. We find that CLM's dense supervision impacts low transformer layers (0-7) far more than MLM does. Freezing low layers during CLM eliminates the downstream benefit; freezing mid layers preserves it. The representational changes persist through the MLM decay phase, even when it matches the CLM phase in length, and they scale with model capacity. We release ModernCamemBERT-bio and ModernBERT-bio as state-of-the-art biomedical encoders in Base and Large sizes.

### [81] [Task-Adaptive Embedding Refinement via Test-time LLM Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12487)
*Ariel Gera,Shir Ashury-Tahan,Gal Bloch,Ohad Eytan,Assaf Toledo*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出LLM引导的查询精炼范式：对于用户输入的原始查询，先在一个小型文档集上通过生成式LLM获取反馈，然后利用该反馈对查询的嵌入表示进行精炼（refine），使嵌入表示能够实时适应目标任务的需求。精炼后的查询嵌入用于后续的搜索或分类任务。

Result: 在多个零样本搜索和分类基准上，该方法在所有测试的嵌入模型和数据集上均取得一致性能提升，相对改进最高达+25%。尤其在文献搜索、意图检测、关键点匹配和细粒度指令遵循任务上效果显著。此外，精炼后的查询能够改善排序质量并在语料中形成更清晰的二分类边界。

Conclusion: 该方法有效扩展了嵌入模型在零样本场景下的适用性，使嵌入模型在无法大规模使用LLM管道的实际部署中成为更具吸引力的替代方案。代码已开源。

Abstract: We explore the effectiveness of an LLM-guided query refinement paradigm for extending the usability of embedding models to challenging zero-shot search and classification tasks. Our approach refines the embedding representation of a user query using feedback from a generative LLM on a small set of documents, enabling embeddings to adapt in real time to the target task. We conduct extensive experiments with state-of-the-art text embedding models across a diverse set of challenging search and classification benchmarks. Empirical results indicate that LLM-guided query refinement yields consistent gains across all models and datasets, with relative improvements of up to +25% in literature search, intent detection, key-point matching, and nuanced query-instruction following. The refined queries improve ranking quality and induce clearer binary separation across the corpus, enabling the embedding space to better reflect the nuanced, task-specific constraints of each ad-hoc user query. Importantly, this expands the range of practical settings in which embedding models can be effectively deployed, making them a compelling alternative when costly LLM pipelines are not viable at corpus-scale. We release our experimental code for reproducibility, at https://github.com/IBM/task-aware-embedding-refinement.

### [82] [LongMemEval-V2: Evaluating Long-Term Agent Memory Toward Experienced Colleagues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12493)
*Di Wu,Zixiang Ji,Asmi Kawatkar,Bryan Kwan,Jia-Chen Gu,Nanyun Peng,Kai-Wei Chang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体记忆基准多聚焦于用户历史、短轨迹或下游任务成功，缺乏对记忆系统是否有效内化环境特定经验的直接评估。LME-V2旨在填补这一空白。

Method: LME-V2基准包含451个问题，覆盖静态状态回忆、动态状态追踪、工作流知识、环境陷阱和前提意识五大记忆能力。提出AgentRunbook-R（基于RAG的知识池方法）和AgentRunbook-C（将轨迹存为文件，调用代码智能体在沙箱中收集证据）两种记忆方法。

Result: AgentRunbook-C以72.5%平均准确率最优，优于最强RAG基线（48.5%）和现成代码智能体基线（69.3%）。但基于代码智能体的方法延迟成本较高。

Conclusion: LME-V2是具有挑战性的长期记忆系统测试基准；AgentRunbook-C推进了准确率-延迟帕累托前沿，但仍存在较大改进空间。

Abstract: Long-term memory is crucial for agents in specialized web environments, where success depends on recalling interface affordances, state dynamics, workflows, and recurring failure modes. However, existing memory benchmarks for agents mostly focus on user histories, short traces, or downstream task success, leaving open how to directly evaluate whether memory systems effectively internalize environment-specific experience. To address this gap, we introduce LongMemEval-V2 (LME-V2), a benchmark for evaluating whether memory systems can help agents acquire the experience needed to become knowledgeable colleagues in customized environments. LME-V2 contains 451 manually curated questions covering five core memory abilities for web agents: static state recall, dynamic state tracking, workflow knowledge, environment gotchas, and premise awareness. Questions are paired with history trajectories containing up to 500 trajectories and 115M tokens. We use a context gathering formulation: memory systems consume history trajectories and return compact evidence for downstream question answering. We propose a suite of two memory methods: AgentRunbook-R, an efficient RAG-based memory with knowledge pools for raw state observations, events, and strategy notes, and AgentRunbook-C, which stores trajectories as files and invokes a coding agent to gather evidence in an augmented sandbox. Experiments show that AgentRunbook-C achieves the best performance with 72.5% average accuracy, outperforming the strongest RAG baseline (48.5%) and the off-the-shelf coding agent baseline (69.3%). Despite the strong performance gains, coding agent based methods have high latency costs. While AgentRunbook-C advances the accuracy-latency Pareto frontier, substantial room for improvement remains. Together, these results establish LME-V2 as a challenging testbed for developing long-term memory systems for environment experience.

### [83] [Sensitivity Analysis of Performance-Based Partitioning in District Heating Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11132)
*Audrey Blizard,Stephanie Stockar*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文对影响区域供热网络分布式控制最优分区的影响因素进行了敏感性分析。基于物理模型的分布式模型预测控制框架和基于性能的分区方法，研究了系统参数变化与最优分区之间的关系，揭示了名义最优分区在扰动工况下的鲁棒性。通过12种参数变化的仿真表明，名义分区在11种情况下平均成本仅增加2.8%，但季节重新分区在需求曲线偏离较大时是必要的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在分析影响区域供热网络分布式控制最优分区的关键因素，研究名义最优分区在参数变化条件下的鲁棒性，为实际工程中的分区设计提供可靠指导。

Method: 采用基于物理模型的分布式模型预测控制框架和基于性能的分区方法，结合学习增强的分支定界法来缩减搜索空间。通过12种参数变化（包括供水温度、运行季节、建筑灵活性、管道特性和建筑类型）进行敏感性分析，使用最优性损失指标评估分区性能。

Result: 名义最优分区在11/12种情况下平均成本仅增加2.8%；3种情况下名义分区在扰动条件下仍为全局最优；但5/12种情况下，案例特定的最优性损失最小化分区表现不如名义分区，原因是热量损失与灵活性成本的相对权重发生了变化。

Conclusion: 成本函数权重和初始条件的适当调优对可靠分区选择至关重要；当需求曲线偏离名义条件较大时（如11月运行案例），应进行季节性重新分区。

Abstract: The paper presents a sensitivity analysis of the factors affecting the optimal partitioning of a district heating network for distributed control. Leveraging a physics-based, distributed model predictive control framework and a performance-based partitioning method, this work studies the relationship between variations in system parameters and the resulting optimal partition, providing insight into the robustness of a nominally designed partition to perturbed operating conditions. The enabling methodology is a learning-enhanced branch and bound method that culls the search space, reducing the number of partitions evaluated for each case. The sensitivity of the nominally optimal partition is characterized across twelve parameter variations, including supply temperature, operating season, building flexibility, pipe characteristics, and building type. This simulation study shows that a well-designed nominal partition exhibits an average cost increase of only 2.8% relative to centralized control across eleven of the twelve cases, with three cases identifying the nominal partition as globally optimal under the perturbed conditions. The robustness study is followed by an analysis of the sensitivity of the optimality loss metric (OLM), revealing that, in five of twelve cases, the case-specific OLM-minimizing partitions underperform the nominally optimal one due to shifts in the relative magnitude of heat loss versus flexibility costs. This indicates that proper tuning of cost function weights and initial conditions for the performance optimization problem is essential for reliable partition selection, and that seasonal repartitioning is warranted when demand profiles deviate substantially from the nominal, as observed in the November operating case.

*Luis A. Garcia-Reyes,Josep Arévalo-Soler,Oriol Gomis-Bellmunt,Eduardo Prieto-Araujo,Vinícius A. Lacerda,Macarena Martin-Almenta,Edgar Nuño-Martínez,Javier Renedo*

The method includes an automated state-interpretation strategy that assigns fitted states to representative control-loop categories based on their dominant frequency ranges, providing an approximate but meaningful physical interpretation of the identified dynamics. This capability allows extensive modal analysis, including eigenvalue sensitivities and participation factors, in systems where internal converter details are unavailable. The methodology is validated on a grid-following (GFL) VSC and applied to the New England system, which contains multiple black-box converters operating in both GFL and grid-forming (GFM) modes. The approach overcomes key limitations of existing identification-based techniques by enabling scalable, interpretable, and system-wide stability assessment.

### [86] [Multi-Agent System Identification with Nonlinear Sheaf Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11204)
*Nivar Anwer,Hans Riess,Matthew Hale*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文研究多智能体系统中局部交互律的恢复问题，指出轨迹数据只能反映节点级聚合效应，无法区分不同交互律。作者证明了恢复的根本障碍是拓扑性的，由sheaf上同调度量，并给出唯一恢复的条件。当障碍非平凡时，有限维参数化类的恢复依赖于数据依赖信息矩阵的正定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从多智能体系统的轨迹数据中恢复局部交互律存在根本性困难，因为轨迹观测仅记录节点状态演化，暴露的是边力的聚合效应，不同交互律在节点层面可能无法区分。作者试图从拓扑角度解释这一障碍。

Method: 利用非线性sheaf Laplacian（图Laplacian的推广）对系统建模，将交互律编码为边势函数；引入sheaf上同调理论分析轨迹数据中交互律的可恢复性；通过信息矩阵的正定性判断有限维参数化类的可恢复条件。

Result: 交互律恢复的根本障碍是拓扑性的，由sheaf上同调度量；上同调消失是唯一恢复的充要条件；当障碍非平凡时，有限维参数化类的可恢复依赖于数据依赖信息矩阵的正定性；实验验证了理论，表明精确复现轨迹并不保证恢复底层交互律。

Conclusion: 轨迹数据对交互律的恢复存在拓扑性障碍，精确复现轨迹不等于恢复真实交互律，需要更丰富的观测或先验知识才能唯一确定。

Abstract: Local interaction laws governing multi-agent systems can be difficult to recover from trajectory data, even when the dynamics are observed faithfully. In systems governed by a nonlinear sheaf Laplacian -- a generalization of the graph Laplacian accommodating heterogeneous state spaces and asymmetric communication channels -- the coordination law is encoded by edge potential functions whose gradients produce the inter-agent forces. Because trajectory observations record node-state evolution, they expose only the aggregate effect of the edge forces at each node: distinct interaction laws that agree at the node level are indistinguishable from trajectory data alone. We show that the fundamental obstruction to recovery is topological, measured by sheaf cohomology, and that unique recovery from an unconstrained function class is possible if and only if this cohomology vanishes. When the obstruction is nontrivial, we show that recovery within a finite-dimensional parameterized class is possible precisely when a data-dependent information matrix is positive definite. Experiments validate the theory and illustrate that accurate trajectory reproduction need not certify recovery of the underlying interaction law.

</details>


### [87] [236 μW Direct-RF PLL-Free Multi-PSK Transmitter Using Oscillator-Based Phase Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11261)

Abstract: This paper presents a compact, low-power, direct RF multi-phase-shift keying (PSK) transmitter (TX) that eliminates the need for a phase-locked loop (PLL) by performing phase modulation directly within a ring oscillator. The proposed architecture exploits synchronized charge extraction at the oscillator's transition points to induce controlled phase shifts while maintaining constant amplitude and frequency. A time-domain multi-triggering technique is introduced to enable reconfigurable multi-mode modulation, supporting 16-PSK, 8-PSK, QPSK, and BPSK within a unified hardware structure. The TX circuit is fabricated in a 22-nm FD-SOI process and operates in the ISM band at 2.4 GHz. Measurement results indicate a symbol rate of 2 MSps with a maximum error vector magnitude (EVM) of 5.13% rms. The core TX occupies 23 {\times} 17.6 μm2 and consumes 236 μW, excluding the output driver, which delivers -10 dBm output power over a 60 MHz bandwidth. The proposed design achieves a favorable trade-off between power consumption, circuit complexity, and modulation flexibility, making it well-suited for low-power wireless applications.

This paper proposes a Lane-Aware Graph Attention Network (LA-GAT) that encodes vehicle interaction within dynamic scene graphs, augmented with a trainable lane-relationship attention bias that prioritizes merge-conflict interactions from the outset of training. ### [95] [Estimation Problems and the Modulating Function Method: The Algebra of Modulating Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12244)
*Davi G. Accioli,Jerome Jouffroy*

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了调制函数的代数性质（封闭性和群性质），提出了一种构造新调制函数的通用算法，并据此构建了对数型和非解析型调制函数族；同时利用调制函数的向量空间与代数结构构造了标准正交调制函数，成功应用于船舶横摇动力学参数估计，避免了矩阵求逆问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 调制函数方法在状态估计、参数估计和故障检测中具有统一性框架，但现有调制函数族结构相似且缺乏系统的代数性质研究，需要形式化其代数结构并提出通用的构造方法。

Method: 首先形式化定义了调制函数的封闭性和群性质；基于这些代数性质提出了一种构造新调制函数的通用算法；利用调制函数构成向量空间和代数的性质，构造标准正交调制函数族。

Result: 构建了对数型调制函数族和3个非解析调制函数族；通过标准正交调制函数成功实现了船舶横摇动力学参数估计，有效避免了矩阵求逆问题。

Conclusion: 调制函数的代数性质为系统构造新调制函数提供了理论基础，标准正交化策略在实际参数估计中具有数值优势。

Abstract: State and parameter estimation, along with fault detection, are three crucial estimation problems within the control systems community. Although different approaches have been proposed for each type of problem, the modulating function method proposes a more unified approach to all three problem classes, being used for state and parameter estimation of lumped systems, fault detection, and estimation of distributed and fractional systems. At the core of the method is the modulating function: a function that evaluates to 0 at the left or right boundaries up to a certain order of derivatives. By selecting the modulating functions, one directly determines the filter characteristics, and, for that reason, different function families have been proposed over the years. Nevertheless, many families of modulating functions are given in a rather similar mathematical structure. In light of these structures, this paper formally discusses the algebraic properties of modulating functions, and, after formalizing the closedness and group properties of modulating functions, a simple algorithm to construct new modulating functions is proposed, discussed, and illustrated with the construction of the newly introduced logarithmic modulating function families and 3 non-analytic modulating function families. Moreover, the fact that total modulating functions form a vector space and an algebra is exploited to construct orthonormal modulating functions, which are then used for the parameter estimation of a boat's roll dynamics, effectively avoiding matrix inversion issues.

TL;DR: 本文分析了无MPC终端代价的Receding Horizon Games，证明了在温和假设下，turnpike现象可推导递归可行性，并给出了实际渐近收敛的充分条件。数值实验表明闭环吸引域随视界长度指数收缩，线性终端惩罚可抑制离开弧并确保渐近收敛到稳态GNE。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Receding Horizon Games通常依赖MPC风格的终端代价（终端约束或终端成本）来保证稳定性和可行性，但这类终端条件在实际中难以设计或过于保守。本文旨在探索在不使用终端代价的情况下，能否仅依靠系统的turnpike性质来保证递归可行性与收敛性。

Method: 1. 理论分析：利用turnpike现象推导无终端代价下的递归可行性；2. 证明实际渐近收敛的充分条件；3. 数值实验：展示闭环吸引域随视界长度指数收缩（类似MPC行为）；4. 引入线性端部惩罚机制，通过数值仿真验证其抑制离开弧、保证渐近收敛的效果。

Result: 1. 在无终端代价下，turnpike现象可保证递归可行性；2. 给出了实际渐近收敛的充分条件；3. 闭环吸引域随视界长度指数收缩（与MPC一致）；4. 线性端部惩罚有效抑制了离开弧，实现了向稳态GNE的渐近收敛。

Conclusion: 无终端代价的Receding Horizon Games在turnpike现象下仍具有递归可行性和实际渐近收敛性，且吸引域指数收缩特性与MPC类似。线性端部惩罚是一种简单有效的改进手段，可弥补无终端代价时的收敛性缺陷。

Abstract: We analyze Receding Horizon Games without any MPC-like terminal ingredients. We show that recursive feasibility can be inferred from the turnpike phenomenon under mild assumptions. Moreover, we prove sufficient conditions for practical asymptotic convergence of the closed-loop trajectories, and we discuss how the gap towards practical asymptotic stability may be closed. We use numerical examples to show that the closed-loop region of attraction around the steady-state GNE shrinks exponentially with the horizon length, a behavior previously known only for model predictive control. Further, we apply a linear end penalty and demonstrate in numerical simulations that it suppresses the leaving arc and ensures asymptotic convergence to the steady-state GNE.

</details>

### [97] [Fused Gromov-Wasserstein Distance with Feature Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12161)
*Harlin Lee,Ying Yu,Mingxin Li,Ranthony Clark*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出带特征选择的融合Gromov-Wasserstein距离（FGW），通过引入自适应特征抑制权重，在保持对齐结构的同时选择性降权或抑制噪声/无关特征，提升高维场景下的可解释性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有FGW距离对所有特征统一对待，在高维场景下大量特征可能是不相关或含噪声的，这限制了模型的可解释性和鲁棒性。

Method: 提出两种特征选择方法：(1) 带Lasso和Ridge惩罚的正则化FGW；(2) 带单纯形约束权重的FGW（含分组扩展）。设计了高效的交替最小化算法，并进行了理论分析（包括边界性质和度量行为）。

Result: 实验表明特征抑制机制增强了可解释性，能揭示任务相关结构，并在计算选区重划等应用中表现良好。

Conclusion: 通过特征选择扩展FGW，在保持联合对齐结构-特征能力的同时，有效提升了模型在高维噪声场景下的可解释性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Fused Gromov-Wasserstein (FGW) distances provide a principled framework for comparing objects by jointly aligning structure and node features. However, existing FGW formulations treat all features uniformly, which limits interpretability and robustness in high-dimensional settings where many features may be irrelevant or noisy. We introduce FGW distances with feature selection, which incorporate adaptive feature suppression weights into the FGW objective to selectively downweight or suppress differentiating features during alignment. We propose two approaches: (1) regularized FGW with Lasso and Ridge penalties, and (2) FGW with simplex-constrained weights, including groupwise extensions. We analyze the resulting models and establish their key theoretical properties, including bounds relative to classical FGW and Gromov-Wasserstein distances, and metric behavior. An efficient alternating minimization algorithm is developed. Experiments illustrate how feature suppression enhances interpretability and reveals task-relevant structure, with a special application to computational redistricting.

### [98] [Enabling Performant and Flexible Model-Internal Observability for LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11093)
*Nengneng Yu,Sixian Xiong,Yibo Zhao,Wei Wang,Zaoxing Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DMI-Lib 是一个高速深度模型检查器，通过异步可观测性子系统实现模型内部状态的高效捕获与导出，在离线批推理和在线服务场景下分别仅引入 0.4%-6.8% 和平均 6% 的性能开销，相比现有方案延迟开销降低 2-15 倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前推理工作负载越来越依赖及时访问模型内部状态，但现有系统缺乏将内部可观测性作为一等基础设施支持的方案，存在性能开销大、与推理优化冲突等问题。

Method: 通过 Ring²（GPU-CPU 内存抽象）实现张量捕获与暂存，结合异步可观测性子系统将观测点与推理热路径解耦，并利用策略控制的主机后端导出数据，在保持服务优化的同时适配多种内部信号与推理后端。

Result: 离线批推理开销仅 0.4%-6.8%，在线服务平均开销 6%，延迟开销相比基线降低 2-15 倍。

Conclusion: DMI-Lib 证明了将内部可观测性作为一等系统原语设计的可行性，能在极低开销下实现丰富的模型内部状态监控，且已开源。

Abstract: Today's inference-time workloads increasingly depend on timely access to a model's internal states. We present DMI-Lib, a high-speed deep model inspector that treats internal observability as a first-class systems primitive, decoupling it from the inference hot path via an asynchronous observability substrate built from Ring^2, a GPU-CPU memory abstraction for capturing and staging tensors, and a policy-controlled host backend that exports them. DMI-Lib enables the placement of observation points across a rich space of internal signals and diverse inference backends while preserving serving optimizations and adhering to tight GPU memory budgets. Our experiments demonstrate that DMI-Lib incurs only 0.4%--6.8% overhead in offline batch inference and an average of 6% in moderate online serving, reducing latency overhead by 2x-15x compared to existing baselines with similar observability features. DMI-Lib is open-sourced at https://github.com/ProjectDMX/DMI.

</details>


### [99] [Newton's Lantern: A Reinforcement Learning Framework for Finetuning AC Power Flow Warm Start Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11102)
*Shourya Bose,Helgi Hilmarsson,Dhruv Suri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Newton's Lantern方法，通过强化学习微调神经求解器，在电力系统潮流计算中实现比传统监督学习方法更优的收敛性和更少的牛顿-拉夫森迭代次数，解决了高负载场景下雅可比矩阵奇异值减小导致的监督学习失效问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有监督学习方法在处理接近电压崩溃的高负载电力系统场景时泛化能力差，作者从理论上证明了当潮流雅可比矩阵的最小奇异值趋近于零时，基于误差大小的监督回归方法会失效，从而揭示了该问题的根本原因。

Method: 提出Newton's Lantern微调流水线：结合组相对策略优化（GRPO）与基于基础模型预测扰动训练的学习奖励模型，以牛顿-拉夫森迭代次数作为监督信号进行优化。

Result: 在IEEE 118节点、GOC 500节点和GOC 2000节点三个基准测试上，Newton's Lantern是唯一在所有测试快照上均收敛的方法，同时实现了最小的平均迭代次数。

Conclusion: 证明了暖启动误差方向比误差大小更关键，并通过强化学习范式有效解决了高负载场景下的收敛问题，为电力系统潮流计算提供了更鲁棒的神经求解方案。

Abstract: Neural warm starts can sharply reduce the number of Newton-Raphson iterations required to solve the AC power flow problem, but existing supervised approaches generalize poorly on heavily loaded instances near voltage collapse. We prove a lower bound on the Newton-Raphson iteration count that depends on the direction of the warm start error rather than on its magnitude, and show as a corollary that the bound becomes vacuous as the smallest singular value of the power-flow Jacobian shrinks, identifying the failure mode of supervised regression near the saddle-node bifurcation. Motivated by this analysis, we introduce Newton's Lantern, a finetuning pipeline that combines group relative policy optimization with a learned reward model trained on perturbations of the base model's predictions, using the iteration count itself as the supervisory signal. Across IEEE 118-bus, GOC 500-bus, and GOC 2000-bus benchmarks, Newton's Lantern is the only method that converges on every test snapshot while attaining the smallest mean iteration count.

</details>


### [100] [Beyond Prediction: Interval Neural Networks for Uncertainty-Aware System Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11460)
*Mehmet Ali Ferah,Tufan Kumbasar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于区间神经网络（INN）的系统辨识框架，通过区间LSTM和区间NODE模型在无概率假设下实现不确定性传播。提出了C-INN（两阶段）和J-INN（单阶段）两种训练策略，实验表明C-INN点预测更准，J-INN区间预测更优，并引入通道弹性概念分析参数不确定性模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统系统辨识方法难以捕捉非线性行为，而深度学习方法虽能建模复杂动力学，却缺乏不确定性量化。本文旨在将深度学习与不确定性量化相结合，构建一个系统性的区间神经网络框架，用于不确定感知的系统辨识。

Method: 提出Interval LSTM和Interval NODE模型，通过区间算术传播不确定性。训练策略包括：C-INN（两阶段，先训练普通NN再转为INN）和J-INN（单阶段联合优化预测精度与区间精度）。采用不确定性感知损失函数和参数化技巧。引入通道弹性概念分析参数层面的不确定性表示。

Result: 在多个系统辨识数据集上：C-INN在点预测精度上表现优异，J-INN在预测区间的准确性和校准度上更优。通道弹性揭示了两种训练策略下模型参数的不同不确定性表示模式。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架有效整合了深度学习与不确定性感知建模，为系统辨识提供了两种各有侧重的实用方案：追求点预测精度选C-INN，追求可靠区间预测选J-INN。

Abstract: System identification (SysID) is critical for modeling dynamical systems from experimental data, yet traditional approaches often fail to capture nonlinear behaviors. While deep learning offers powerful tools for modeling such dynamics, incorporating uncertainty quantification is essential to ensure reliable predictions. This paper presents a systematic framework for constructing and training interval Neural Networks (INNs) for uncertainty-aware SysID. By extending crisp neural networks into interval counterparts, we develop Interval LSTM and NODE models that propagate uncertainty through interval arithmetic without probabilistic assumptions. This design allows them to represent uncertainty and produce prediction intervals. For training, we propose two strategies: Cascade INN (C-INN), a two-stage approach converting a trained crisp NN into an INN, and Joint INN (J-INN), a one-stage framework jointly optimizing prediction accuracy and interval precision. Both strategies employ uncertainty-aware loss functions and parameterization tricks to ensure reliable learning. Comprehensive experiments on multiple SysID datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of both approaches and benchmark their performance against well-established uncertainty-aware baselines: C-INN achieves superior point prediction accuracy, whereas J-INN yields more accurate and better-calibrated prediction intervals. Furthermore, to reveal how uncertainty is represented across model parameters, the concept of channel-wise elasticity is introduced, which is used to identify distinct patterns across the two training strategies. The results of this study demonstrate that the proposed framework effectively integrates deep learning with uncertainty-aware modeling.

</details>


### [101] [Muon is Not That Special: Random or Inverted Spectra Work Just as Well](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11181)
*Zakhar Shumaylov,Nathaël Da Costa,Peter Zaika,Bálint Mucsányi,Alex Massucco,Yoav Gelberg,Carola-Bibiane Schönlieb,Yarin Gal,Philipp Hennig*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过提出Freon（基于Schatten拟范数的优化器族）和Kaon（用随机噪声替代奇异值的优化器），证明优化性能的关键不在于精确的几何结构，而在于对齐（alignment）和下降势（descent potential）两个局部量。Muon优化器的成功源于其步长最优性，而非全局几何结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质疑Muon优化器成功的"几何叙事"——即其性能来源于非欧几何结构（如与二阶方法相似性或线性最小化预言机理论），试图证明精确的几何结构并非影响优化性能的关键因素。

Method: 1) 提出Freon优化器族，基于Schatten（拟）范数，采用QDWH迭代近似，可在SGD和Muon之间插值并外推至拟范数区域；2) 提出Kaon优化器，用随机噪声替代奇异值，完全抛弃几何结构；3) 在随机特征模型中分析对齐与下降势两个局部量，解释优化器性能差异。

Result: 1) GPT-2上最优的Schatten参数严格位于拟范数区域，无法被任何酉不变LMO表示；2) Kaon（无几何结构）在性能上与Muon持平，且保留经典收敛保证；3) 优化性能主要由对齐和下降势两个局部量控制。

Conclusion: Muon的成功并非源于追踪理想的全局几何结构，而是通过保证步长最优性（步长自适应）来实现。精确的几何结构在实践中是不必要的。

Abstract: The recent empirical success of the Muon optimizer has renewed interest in non-Euclidean optimization, typically justified by similarities with second-order methods, and linear minimization oracle (LMO) theory. In this paper, we challenge this geometric narrative through three contributions, demonstrating that precise geometric structure is not the key factor affecting optimization performance. First, we introduce Freon, a family of optimizers based on Schatten (quasi-)norms, powered by a novel, provably optimal QDWH-based iterative approximation. Freon naturally interpolates between SGD and Muon, while smoothly extrapolating into the quasi-norm regime. Empirically, the best-performing Schatten parameters for GPT-2 lie strictly within the quasi-norm regime, and thus cannot be represented by any unitarily invariant LMO. Second, noting that Freon performs well across a wide range of exponents, we introduce Kaon, an absurd optimizer that replaces singular values with random noise. Despite lacking any coherent geometric structure, Kaon matches Muon's performance and retains classical convergence guarantees, proving that strict adherence to a precise geometry is practically irrelevant. Third, having shown that geometry is not the primary driver of performance, we demonstrate it is instead controlled by two local quantities: alignment and descent potential. Ultimately, each optimizer must tune its step size around these two quantities. While their dynamics are difficult to predict a-priori, evaluating them within a stochastic random feature model yields a precise insight: Muon succeeds not by tracking an ideal global geometry, but by guaranteeing step-size optimality.

</details>


### [102] [Extending Kernel Trick to Influence Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11239)
*Zhenhuan Sun,Shahrokh Valaee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种影响函数的对偶表示，其计算复杂度随数据集大小而非模型大小扩展，适用于模型规模远大于数据集规模的场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统影响函数的计算复杂度随模型大小扩展，当模型规模很大时难以高效计算。作者希望提出一种在模型规模远大于数据集规模时更高效的影响函数计算方法。

Method: 提出影响函数的对偶表示，将计算复杂度从依赖模型大小转为依赖数据集大小。该方法仅适用于可线性化模型（训练过程中行为可由线性化近似），且需要实例化一个大小随模型输出维度与数据集大小乘积增长的矩阵。

Result: 理论和实验均表明，在模型规模远大于数据集规模时，对偶表示可作为原始影响函数的高效替代方案，用于估计移除数据点后的参数变化、模型输出和损失变化。

Conclusion: 对偶表示在特定条件下（模型大、数据集小、模型可线性化）是原始影响函数的有效替代，但其适用范围受限于可线性化模型和矩阵存储开销。

Abstract: In this paper, we present a dual representation of the influence functions, whose computational complexity scales with dataset size rather than model size. Both analytically and experimentally, we show that this representation can be an efficient alternative to the original influence functions for estimating changes in parameters, model outputs and loss due to data point removal, when model size is large relative to dataset size, or when evaluating the original influence functions in parameter space is infeasible. The dual representation, however, is limited to linearizable models, which are models whose behavior can be approximated by their linearizations throughout training, and requires materializing a matrix, whose size grows with the product of model output dimension and dataset size.

### [103] [Couple to Control: Joint Initial Noise Design in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11311)
*Jing Jia,Liyue Shen,Guanyang Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将扩散模型的初始噪声从独立采样扩展到耦合设计，通过保持边缘高斯分布但引入样本间依赖关系，在不增加采样成本的情况下提升生成多样性和质量。实验表明，排斥性高斯耦合可在SD1.5/SDXL/SD3上提升多样性，子空间耦合支持固定物体背景生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型传统上使用独立高斯噪声初始化，但作者认为这种独立性假设只是更广泛的有效联合噪声设计中的一种选择。通过设计噪声间的耦合结构，可以在不改变预训练模型输入分布的情况下控制生成样本间的关系。

Method: 提出将初始噪声从独立采样改为耦合设计框架，保持每个噪声边缘为标准高斯分布（不改变预训练模型输入分布），而样本间的依赖结构可人为设计。具体包括排斥性高斯耦合（提升多样性）和子空间耦合（支持固定物体背景生成），且可作为优化管道的结构化初始化。

Result: 在SD1.5、SDXL、SD3上，排斥性高斯耦合在保持提示对齐和图像质量的同时提升了图库多样性，以相同采样成本匹配或超越了测试时噪声优化基线。子空间耦合在固定物体背景生成任务中产生多样自然的背景，优于专用修补基线，且前景保真度可调。

Conclusion: 初始噪声耦合设计是一个通用框架，涵盖多种现有方法作为特例。耦合噪声可以独立提升生成质量（无额外计算成本），也可作为优化管道的结构化初始化（有额外计算时）。该框架为扩散模型的初始噪声控制提供了新的设计空间。

Abstract: Diffusion models typically generate image batches from independent Gaussian initial noises. We argue that this independence assumption is only one choice within a broader class of valid joint noise designs. Instead, one can specify a coupling of the initial noises: each noise remains marginally standard Gaussian, so the pretrained diffusion model receives the same single-sample input distribution, while the dependence across samples is chosen by design. This reframes initial-noise control from selecting or optimizing individual seeds to designing the dependence structure of a multi-sample gallery. This view gives a general framework for initial-noise design, covering several existing methods as special cases and leading naturally to new coupled-noise constructions. Coupled noise can improve generation on its own without adding sampling cost, and it is flexible enough to serve as a structured initialization for optimization-based pipelines when additional computation is available. Empirically, repulsive Gaussian coupling improves gallery diversity on SD1.5, SDXL, and SD3 while largely preserving prompt alignment and image quality. It matches or outperforms recent test-time noise-optimization baselines on several diversity metrics at the same sampling cost as independent generation. Subspace couplings also support fixed-object background generation, producing diverse, natural backgrounds compared with specialized inpainting baselines, with a tunable trade-off in foreground fidelity.

</details>


### [104] [Quotient-Categorical Representations for Bellman-Compatible Average-Reward Distributional Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11289)
*Ege C. Kaya,Aliasghar Pourghani,Vijay Gupta,Abolfazl Hashemi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对平均奖励强化学习中的增益与偏差估计问题，提出了一种商空间-分类参数化框架，定义了投影平均奖励分布算子，证明了其良定义性、非扩张性及不动点存在性，并在理想化设定下证明了TD更新的几乎必然收敛性和有限迭代残差界，以及耦合增益估计器的非扩张性与马尔可夫收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平均奖励强化学习中，增益（gain）和偏差（bias）的估计至关重要，但偏差仅定义到加法常数。这使得在实数直线上直接进行分布类比（distributional analogues）是病态的（ill-posed）。作者希望建立一套在商空间上良定义的分布强化学习理论框架。

Method: 1) 提出商空间（quotient-space）公式化，将状态索引的偏差律（bias law）视为在同一平移下等价；2) 引入尊重该对称性的分类参数化（categorical parameterization）；3) 在商-分类空间上定义投影平均奖励分布算子，证明其良定义性、在坐标Cramér度量下非扩张且存在不动点；4) 研究采样递归，其平均场映射为该算子的异步松弛；5) 在理想化中心奖励设定下分析单状态TD更新的收敛性与残差界；6) 当增益未知时，耦合在线增益估计器并证明非扩张性与马尔可夫收敛性；7) 分析同步精确更新在商定律层面的增益无关性。

Result: 1) 证明了投影平均奖励分布算子是良定义且非扩张的，存在不动点；2) 在理想化中心奖励设定下，单状态TD更新几乎必然收敛，且具有有限迭代残差界（独立同分布和马尔可夫采样下均成立）；3) 耦合增益估计器的方案保持非扩张性，且马尔可夫采样下收敛；4) 同步精确更新在商定律层面与增益无关，揭示了理想商分布与实用固定网格分类表示之间的结构性差异。

Conclusion: 本文为平均奖励强化学习中的分布方法建立了严谨的理论基础，解决了偏差估计的平移不变性带来的病态问题，证明了关键算子的性质和收敛性，并揭示了理论理想框架与实际分类表示之间的结构性差异，为后续分布平均奖励RL算法设计提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Average-reward reinforcement learning requires estimating the gain and the bias, which is defined only up to an additive constant. This makes direct distributional analogues ill-posed on the real line. We introduce a quotient-space formulation in which state-indexed bias laws are identified up to a common translation, together with a categorical parameterization that respects this symmetry. On this quotient-categorical space, we define a projected average-reward distributional operator and show that it is well-defined, non-expansive in a coordinate Cramér metric, and admits fixed points. We then study sampled recursions whose mean-field maps are asynchronous relaxations of this operator. In an idealized centered-reward setting, a one-state temporal-difference update enjoys almost sure convergence together with finite-iteration residual bounds under both i.i.d. and Markovian sampling. When the gain is unknown, we augment the recursion with an online gain estimator, and prove non-expansiveness and Markovian convergence of the resulting coupled scheme. Finally, we show that synchronous exact updates are gain-independent at the quotient-law level, isolating a structural contrast between ideal quotient distributions and practical fixed-grid categorical representations.

</details>


### [105] [$\varepsilon$-Good Action Identification in Fixed-Budget Monte Carlo Tree Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11324)
*Yinan Li,Tuan Nguyen,Kwang-Sung Jun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了深度为2的最大-最小树中的固定预算最大-最小行动识别问题，提出了一种无需输入ε的ε-agnostic算法，并给出了误识别概率的指数级衰减界，这是首个固定预算下的可证明算法保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受近似规划启发，我们关注ε-好子树识别问题。在实际应用中，找到精确最优解往往代价过高，因此允许一定近似误差ε的识别更具实用价值。

Method: 提出了一种ε-agnostic算法，该算法不需要用户指定ε作为输入，但能对每个有意义的ε都能达到实例相关的误差界。算法分析利用H₂(ε)捕获了子树间和子树内的差距结构。

Result: 误识别概率衰减为exp(-Θ̃(T/H₂(ε)))。当每个子树只有一个叶子时，问题退化为标准固定预算最优臂识别，分析恢复并改进了已知的ε-好保证。同时给出了最大-最小识别与标准K臂老虎机不同难度结构的下界结果。

Conclusion: 这是首个固定预算最大-最小行动识别的可证明算法保证，揭示了该问题与标准多臂老虎机问题在难度结构上的本质差异。

Abstract: We study the fixed-budget max-min action identification problem in depth-2 max-min trees, an important special case of Monte Carlo Tree Search. A learner sequentially allocates $T$ samples to leaves and then recommends a subtree whose minimum leaf value is largest. Motivated by approximate planning, we focus on $\varepsilon$-good subtree identification, where any subtree whose min value is within $\varepsilon$ of the optimal maximin value is acceptable.
  Our main contribution is an $\varepsilon$-agnostic algorithm: it does not require $\varepsilon$ as input, but achieves instance-dependent error bounds for every meaningful $\varepsilon$. We show that the misidentification probability decays as $\exp(-\widetildeΘ(T/H_2(\varepsilon)))$, where $H_2(\varepsilon)$ captures both cross-subtree and within-subtree gaps. When each subtree has a single leaf, the problem reduces to standard fixed-budget best-arm identification, and our analysis recovers, up to accelerating factors, known $\varepsilon$-good guarantees for halving-style methods while giving a new $\varepsilon$-good guarantee for Successive Rejects.
  On the lower-bound side, we provide complementary positive and negative results showing that max-min identification has a different hardness structure from standard $K$-armed bandits. To our knowledge, this is the first provable fixed-budget algorithmic guarantee for max-min action identification.

### [106] [Error whitening: Why Gauss-Newton outperforms Newton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11316)
*Maricela Best McKay,Nathan P. Lawrence,Brian Wetton,R. Bhushan Gopaluni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从函数空间视角分析，发现广义高斯-牛顿（GGN）矩阵将牛顿方向投影到模型切空间，去除了参数化带来的扭曲（误差白化效应），从而解释为何高斯-牛顿下降法优于牛顿法，并在监督学习、物理信息深度学习、近似动态规划中实证优于牛顿法、Adam和Muon。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管高斯-牛顿矩阵被视为海森矩阵的半正定近似，但实验表明高斯-牛顿下降法优于牛顿法，这一反直觉现象缺乏理论解释。

Method: 从函数空间视角分析，证明GGN矩阵将牛顿方向投影到模型切空间，而仅含雅可比矩阵的变体将损失梯度投影到同一空间。这消除了参数化带来的扭曲，用恒等矩阵替代了JJ^⊤，作者将该效应称为"误差白化"。

Result: 在监督学习、物理信息深度学习、近似动态规划等案例中，高斯-牛顿优化器遵循理论预测的函数空间动态，优于牛顿法、Adam和Muon。

Conclusion: 误差白化是高斯-牛顿下降法的特有性质，使其与牛顿法从根本上区分开来，解释了其在实践中优于牛顿法的原因。

Abstract: The Gauss-Newton matrix is widely viewed as a positive semidefinite approximation of the Hessian, yet mounting empirical evidence shows that Gauss-Newton descent outperforms Newton's method. We adopt a function space perspective to analyze this phenomenon. We show that the generalized Gauss-Newton (GGN) matrix projects the Newton direction in function space onto the model's tangent space, while a Jacobian-only variant obtained by applying the least squares Gauss-Newton matrix to non-least squares losses projects the function space loss gradient onto this same tangent space. Both projections eliminate distortions from the model's parameterization. Specifically, the evolution of the prediction-target mismatch depends on the model's parameterization through the matrix $JJ^\top$ where $J$ is the Jacobian of the model with respect to its parameters. The projections effectively replace $JJ^\top$ with the identity. We call this effect error whitening. Once the parameterization is removed, the prediction-target mismatch evolves according to dynamics dictated by the structure of the loss and the projection produced by the optimizer. Error whitening is a special property of Gauss-Newton descent that rigorously distinguishes it from Newton's method. We empirically demonstrate that Gauss-Newton optimizers follow the theoretically predicted function space dynamics and outperforms Newton's method, Adam, and Muon across case studies spanning supervised learning, physics-informed deep learning, and approximate dynamic programming.

At the same time, fairness in temporal contexts, particularly survival/time-to-event (TTE) analysis, remains relatively underexplored, with current approaches to fair survival analysis adopting statistical fairness definitions, which, even with unlimited data, cannot disentangle the causal mechanisms that generate disparities. To address this gap, we develop a causal framework for fairness in TTE analysis, enabling the decomposition of disparities in survival into contributions from direct, indirect, and spurious pathways. This provides a human-understandable explanation of why disparities arise and how they evolve over time. Our non-parametric approach proceeds in four steps: (1) formalizing the necessary assumptions about censoring and lack of confounding using a graphical model; (2) recovering the conditional survival function given covariates; (3) applying the Causal Reduction Theorem to reframe the problem in a form amenable to causal pathway decomposition; (4) estimating the effects efficiently. Finally, our approach is used to analyze the temporal evolution of racial disparities in outcome after admission to an intensive care unit (ICU).

### [109] [Gradient Clipping Beyond Vector Norms: A Spectral Approach for Matrix-Valued Parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11838)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有梯度裁剪将所有参数视为向量，忽略了神经网络参数的矩阵结构；实际中发现数据异常值只会放大梯度矩阵中少数前导奇异值，而其余谱几乎不变，因此需要一种保留矩阵结构的裁剪方法。

Method: 提出频谱裁剪，对梯度矩阵中超过阈值的奇异值进行钳制，同时保留奇异方向；引入基于移动平均或滑动窗口分位数的自适应阈值；采用随机截断SVD只裁剪前r个奇异值以降低计算开销。

Result: 在非凸优化下证明了带有频谱裁剪的SGD在重尾噪声下达到最优收敛速率$O(K^{\frac{2-2α}{3α-2}})$；在合成重尾数据和神经网络训练任务中表现优于基线方法。

Conclusion: 频谱裁剪统一了经典范数裁剪，更有效地应对重尾噪声和异常值，且易于集成到现有优化器中，具备理论和实践的双重优势。

Abstract: Gradient clipping is a standard safeguard for training neural networks under noisy, heavy-tailed stochastic gradients; yet, most clipping rules treat all parameters as vectors and ignore the matrix structure of modern architectures. We show empirically that data outliers often amplify only a small number of leading singular values in layer-wise gradient matrices, while the rest of the spectrum remains largely unchanged. Motivated by this phenomenon, we propose spectral clipping, which stabilizes training by clamping singular values that exceed a threshold while preserving the singular directions. This framework generalizes classical gradient norm clipping and can be easily integrated into existing optimizers. We provide a convergence analysis for non-convex optimization with spectrally clipped SGD, yielding the optimal $\mathcal{O}\left(K^{\frac{2 - 2α}{3α- 2}}\right)$ rate for heavy-tailed noise. To minimize hyperparameter tuning, we introduce layer-wise adaptive thresholds based on moving averages or sliding-window quantiles of the top singular values. Finally, we develop efficient implementations that clip only the top $r$ singular values via randomized truncated SVD, avoiding full decompositions for large layers. We demonstrate competitive performance across synthetic heavy-tailed settings and neural network training tasks.

### [110] [Adaptive Calibration in Non-Stationary Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11490)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线预测算法多聚焦于完全对抗环境，导致在更温和的场景（如近平稳）下表现保守。核心问题是：能否设计出校准误差自动适应环境非平稳程度的算法，在i.i.d.和对抗之间平滑过渡？

Method: 提出基于epoch调度的学习框架，结合预测空间的非均匀划分——在真实均值附近分配更细的粒度。针对三种校准度量（ℓ1、ℓ2、伪KL）分别设计了自适应算法，其中非平稳度C由最小ℓ1均值偏差衡量且未知。

Result: ℓ1校准误差达到Õ(√T + (TC)^{1/3})，ℓ2和伪KL校准误差均达到Õ((1+C)^{1/3})。这些界在平稳时匹配最优，在完全对抗时恢复已知保证。

Conclusion: 成功回答了如何自适应非平稳环境的问题，算法在理论和实际间实现了更优雅的权衡，为在线预测的稳健性和适应性提供了新框架。

Abstract: Making calibrated online predictions is a central challenge in modern AI systems. Much of the existing literature focuses on fully adversarial environments where outcomes may be arbitrary, leading to conservative algorithms that can perform suboptimally in more benign settings, such as when outcomes are nearly stationary. This gap raises a natural question: can we design online prediction algorithms whose calibration error automatically adapts to the degree of non-stationarity in the environment, smoothly interpolating between i.i.d. and adversarial regimes? We answer this question in the affirmative and develop a suite of algorithms that achieve adaptive calibration guarantees under multiple calibration measures. Specifically, with $T$ being the number of rounds and $C\in[0,T]$ being an unknown non-stationary measure defined as the minimal $\ell_1$ deviation of the mean outcomes, our algorithms attain $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T}+(TC)^{\frac{1}{3}})$ for $\ell_1$ calibration error and $\widetilde{O}((1+C)^{\frac{1}{3}})$ for both $\ell_2$ and pseudo KL calibration error. These bounds match the optimal rates in the stationary case ($C=0$) and recover known guarantees in the fully adversarial regime ($C=T$). Our approach builds on and extends prior work [Hu et al., 2026, Luo et al., 2025], introducing an epoch-based scheduling together with a novel non-uniform partition of the prediction space that allocates finer resolution near the underlying ground truth.

In this paper, we propose Heavy Tailed Activation Function (HTAF), a smooth approximation to the Heaviside function that enables stable training with gradient-based optimization. We construct HTAF as a sigmoid hyperbolic tangent composite function and theoretically show that it maintains a large gradient mass around zero inputs while exhibiting slower gradient decay in the tail regions.
