  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双层优化中下层可行集为固定多面体时存在两大挑战：(1) 活动集变化导致上层目标非光滑；(2) 现有超梯度方法需要计算下层Hessian逆或等价线性求解，计算成本高昂。

Method: 采用对数障碍函数平滑下层问题，得到可微的代理目标；开发仅需上层和下层目标梯度的代理梯度算法，其二阶项仅为固定多面体约束决定的显式对数障碍Hessian；引入局部Dikin几何分析，利用障碍度量提供无需先知(Oracle)的曲率尺度，设计屏障感知的步长调度以保持迭代在局部良态区域。

Result: 在确定环境下取得~O(K^{-2/3})的平稳性收敛率；在上层仅有界随机噪声下取得~O(K^{-2/5})的收敛率；同时对屏障参数衰减下的偏差进行了定量控制。

Conclusion: 本文通过障碍平滑和Dikin几何分析，有效解决了多面体约束双层优化中的非光滑性和计算复杂性问题，为这类问题提供了一种高效且理论保证完备的求解方案。

Abstract: We study bilevel optimization with a fixed polyhedral lower feasible set. Such problems are challenging for two reasons: active-set changes can make the upper objective nonsmooth, and existing hypergradient methods typically require lower-Hessian inversions or equivalent linear solves, which are computationally expensive. To address these issues, we adopt a logarithmic barrier smoothing of the lower problem to obtain a differentiable approximation of the constrained bilevel objective, and develop a proxy-gradient algorithm for the resulting barrier-smoothed surrogate. The algorithm uses only gradients of the upper and lower objectives; its only second-order object is the explicit logarithmic barrier Hessian determined by the fixed polyhedral constraints. Barrier smoothing restores differentiability, but Euclidean smoothness constants are not uniformly bounded near the boundary. We therefore develop a local Dikin-geometry analysis in which the barrier-metric provides an oracle-free curvature scale near the moving lower centers. This leads to barrier-aware schedules that keep the iterates inside locally well-behaved regions. For the barrier-smoothed objective, we prove stationarity rates of $\widetilde{O}(K^{-2/3})$ in the deterministic setting and $\widetilde{O}(K^{-2/5})$ under upper-level-only bounded stochastic noise after $K$ outer iterations, together with quantitative bias control as the barrier parameter decreases.

</details>


### [165] [Efficient and provably convergent end-to-end training of deep neural networks with linear constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11526)
*Zonglin Yang,Zhexuan Gu,Yancheng Yuan*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多数据驱动应用需要在深度神经网络中引入线性约束（如通过投影层），但现有缺乏严格的数学理论和高效反向传播算法，主要难点在于投影层解映射的非光滑性阻碍了梯度计算。

Method: 提出投影层的HS-Jacobian（可高效计算），证明其对多面体集投影算子是保守映射（conservative mapping），从而可无缝集成到非光滑自动微分框架中，支持Adam等优化器进行端到端训练。

Result: 建立了基于HS-Jacobian的Adam算法在带线性约束深度神经网络训练中的收敛保证；在金融、计算机视觉、网络架构设计等任务上的实验表明该方法优于现有流行方法。

Conclusion: HS-Jacobian有效解决了投影层非光滑带来的反向传播难题，为带线性约束的深度神经网络端到端训练提供了理论与算法基础，并在实际应用中展现了优越性能。

Abstract: Training a deep neural network with the outputs of selected layers satisfying linear constraints is required in many contemporary data-driven applications. While this can be achieved by incorporating projection layers into the neural network, its end-to-end training remains challenging due to the lack of rigorous theory and efficient algorithms for backpropagation. A key difficulty in developing the theory and efficient algorithms for backpropagation arose from the nonsmoothness of the solution mapping of the projection layer. To address this bottleneck, we introduce an efficiently computable HS-Jacobian to the projection layer. Importantly, we prove that the HS-Jacobian is a conservative mapping for the projection operator onto the polyhedral set, enabling its seamless integration into the nonsmooth automatic differentiation framework for backpropagation. Therefore, many efficient algorithms, such as Adam, can be applied for end-to-end training of deep neural networks with linear constraints. Particularly, we establish convergence guarantees of the HS-Jacobian based Adam algorithm for training linearly constrained deep neural networks. Extensive experiment results on several important applications, including finance, computer vision, and network architecture design, demonstrate the superior performance of our method compared to other existing popular methods.

Abstract: Efficient methods for non-convex black-box optimization largely rely on sampling. In this context, the Zeroth-Order Proximal Operator (ZOPO) and the corresponding Zeroth-Order Proximal Point Algorithm (ZOPPA) have attracted significant interest, as they combine the advantage of requiring only objective evaluations with the powerful theoretical framework of proximal point algorithms. ZOPO depends on a temperature parameter which, when going to zero, reduces ZOPO to the exact proximal operator. By exploiting this property, the vanishing-temperature regime has been leveraged in several works to obtain theoretical guarantees via inexact proximal methods. However, this regime is computationally unsustainable when sampling is used to estimate ZOPO, since the corresponding Monte Carlo estimators suffer from severe variance issues. We therefore propose a comprehensive analysis of ZOPO for any fixed positive temperature, and prove convergence of ZOPPA under minimal assumptions on the objective function. We do so by demonstrating that ZOPPA can be interpreted as an exact proximal point method applied to an auxiliary smoothed objective, rather than an inexact method on the original function. Importantly, we further derive explicit guarantees connecting this smoothed problem back to the original objective and establish convergence results for the sampled method (S-ZOPPA) at a fixed temperature.

Abstract: This paper addresses the practical challenge in Entropic Optimal Transport (EOT) where the underlying ground cost function is typically latent and unobserved. ### [170] [Securing the Flow: Maritime Energy Resilience under Correlated and Decision-Dependent Disruptions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11990)
*Monit Sharma,Hoong Chuin Lau*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个两阶段随机多商品流模型，用于设计在相关咽喉点中断下的弹性海上能源供应网络。模型考虑了中断相关性、决策依赖的情景概率和均值-CVaR风险目标，并通过Benders分解等算法求解。基于印度能源进口数据的实证表明，随机解价值为14.8%，决策依赖概率价值为0.93%-8.18%，且发现网络具有结构性联合故障韧性，LPG是最脆弱的商品，而原油可通过储备和管道完全对冲。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 海上能源运输咽喉点（如霍尔木兹海峡、曼德海峡）的中断会对能源安全构成严重威胁。传统模型假设中断独立或概率固定，忽略了相邻咽喉点同时失效的相关性以及基础设施使用程度对中断风险的反馈效应。因此，需要一种能够捕捉相关中断、风险暴露反馈和尾部风险的新模型来指导韧性网络设计。

Method: 构建两阶段随机多商品流模型：第一阶段决策战略储备和基础设施激活，第二阶段在相关中断场景下进行路由优化。三个关键特征：相关中断场景（联合失效）、通过仿射扭曲实现决策依赖的情景概率（利用暴露程度影响风险）、均值-CVaR目标缓解尾部短缺。方法上，决策依赖概率通过McCormick线性化转化为精确MILP，CVaR保持场景可分解性，Benders分解结合基于走廊的群体失效割实现有限收敛。

Result: 基于印度海上能源进口数据（16节点、28弧）的校准结果表明：Benders分解在|S|=729场景下以恒定迭代次数（10-11）恢复最优解；随机解价值（VSS）为14.8%；决策依赖概率价值（VEP）为0.93%-8.18%；均值-CVaR前沿在置信水平α≈0.75处存在设计相变；值得注意的是，建模相关性的价值在压力测试中为零，表明网络组合已通过相同对冲机制吸收联合走廊中断；LPG是最脆弱的商品，原油可通过储备和管道完全对冲。

Conclusion: 该模型有效解决了相关咽喉点中断下的韧性网络设计问题。核心发现是网络具有结构性联合故障韧性——由于多元化的组合策略，联合中断并不比单一中断需要不同的对冲机制。研究强调了决策依赖风险暴露的重要性，并为不同能源商品的脆弱性差异提供了洞见，对印度等能源进口大国的战略储备规划具有指导意义。

Abstract: We develop a two-stage stochastic multi-commodity flow model to design a resilient maritime energy supply network under correlated chokepoint disruptions. A planner selects strategic inventories and infrastructure activations prior to uncertainty resolution, then routes crude oil, LNG, LPG, and fertilizer through a capacitated network. Three features distinguish this model: disruption scenarios are \emph{correlated}, reflecting the reality that proximate chokepoints (e.g., Hormuz, Bab el-Mandeb) fail jointly; scenario probabilities depend endogenously on first-stage decisions via affine distortion, formalizing \emph{risk exposure through utilization}; and a mean-CVaR objective mitigates tail-risk shortages. Methodologically, the decision-dependent probability model admits an exact MILP reformulation via McCormick linearization. CVaR preserves scenario-wise decomposability, and our Benders decomposition with corridor-based group-failure cuts converges finitely. The model is calibrated to Indian maritime energy imports (16 nodes, 28 arcs) using EIA, UNCTAD, World Bank, and operational data from the 2026 Hormuz crisis. Benders recovers the extensive-form optimum for scenario sizes up to $|S|=729$ with a constant iteration count (10-11). Empirically, the value of the stochastic solution (VSS) is 14.8%; the value of decision-dependent probabilities (VEP) ranges from 0.93% to 8.18%. The mean-CVaR frontier exhibits a design phase transition at confidence level $α\approx 0.75$. Notably, the value of modeling correlation is identically zero across stress tests: the network's diversified portfolio absorbs joint-corridor disruptions using the same hedging mechanisms as single-corridor disruptions (\emph{structural joint-failure resilience}). Finally, LPG emerges as the most exposed commodity, whereas crude oil is fully hedgeable via reserves and pipeline bypasses.

The governing equation here consists of evolution and the damping part. Existence of solutions is established within the framework of maximal monotone operators where one first proves that the evolution operator is a linear skew-adjoint operator and the distributed damping term is a Nemytskii relation which is then proven to be maximal monotone. Maximal monotonicity of the combined operator is then a consequence of Rockafellar's theorem. Furthermore, we propose a novel funnel control design that ensures the angular velocity of the drill bit follows a dynamically adjusted reference trajectory, while the tracking error remains confined within a pre-specified performance funnel. The reference adjustment mechanism adapts in response to large wave traveling times that may cause performance degradation. The corresponding feasibility result is illustrated by some simulations.

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种四元数域内的矩-四元数-平方和（QSOS）层次结构，用于求解四元数多项式优化问题。该层次结构由一系列半定规划（SDP）松弛组成，提供单调递增的下界。通过引入相关稀疏性和增强型松弛，显著提升了大规模问题的可扩展性和紧致性，数值实验验证了其在计算效率和精度上的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有四元数优化方法多依赖四元数到实数的转换，导致问题规模膨胀；传统SDP松弛计算开销大，难以处理大规模稀疏问题。本文旨在直接在四元数域构建优化框架，以提升效率和可扩展性。

Method: 提出四元数域内的QSOS层次结构（三明治结构：矩-四元数-平方和），生成单调下界的SDP松弛序列；引入相关稀疏性利用问题稀疏结构降低SDP规模；提出增强型QSOS松弛，通过可控方式扩大单项式基以提高紧致性。

Result: 数值实验表明，所提方法在保持与现有方法相当精度的前提下，显著降低了计算时间和内存占用；在四元数最大边界准则问题和经典方向同步问题中验证了实际有效性。

Conclusion: 本文构建了直接在四元数域求解多项式优化问题的完整框架，通过稀疏性利用和松弛增强策略，在精度与效率间取得了良好平衡，为四元数优化领域的实际应用提供了可行方案。

Abstract: This paper introduces a Moment-Quaternion-Sum-of-Squares (QSOS) hierarchy for solving a class of quaternion polynomial optimization problems. This hierarchy is formulated directly in the quaternion domain and consists of a sequence of semidefinite programming (SDP) relaxations that provide monotonic lower bounds on the optimal value. To improve scalability, we incorporate correlative sparsity, which can significantly reduce the size of the resulting SDPs for large-scale sparse problems. Furthermore, we introduce a strengthened QSOS relaxation, which enhances the tightness of the standard relaxation by enlarging the monomial basis in a controlled manner. Our various Numerical experiments show that our approach provides comparable bounds to existing approaches, while significantly reducing computation time and memory usage. In particular, applications to the quaternion-based maximum margin criterion problem and the classical orientation synchronization problem illustrate the practical effectiveness of the framework.

</details>


### [174] [Convergence Analysis of Hessian-Damped Tikhonov Regularized Dynamics with Oscillation Control for Convex-Concave Bilinear Saddle Point Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12223)
*Bohan Zhang,Xiaojun Zhang*

Main category: math.OC

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一类包含五个时变参数（粘性阻尼、时间缩放、外推、Tikhonov正则化、Hessian驱动阻尼）的广义二阶原始-对偶动力系统，通过构造Lyapunov函数分析渐近收敛性。

Result: 获得了原始-对偶间隙的收敛率与轨迹有界性，给出了积分估计；理论上证明了轨迹强收敛到最小范数解，并验证了Hessian驱动阻尼对振荡的缓解作用；数值实验验证了理论结果。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a class of general second-order primal-dual dynamical systems with Tikhonov regularization and Hessian-driven damping for solving convex-concave bilinear saddle point problems. The proposed dynamical system incorporates five general time-varying terms: viscous damping, time scaling, extrapolation, Tikhonov regularization, and Hessian-driven damping parameters. Under suitable parametric conditions, we analyze the asymptotic convergence properties of the dynamical system by constructing appropriate Lyapunov functions. Specifically, we obtain the convergence rate of the primal-dual gap and the boundedness of trajectories in the proposed dynamical system, and provide some integral estimates. Furthermore, we theoretically prove that the trajectories generated by the dynamical system converge strongly to the minimum-norm solution of the saddle point problem, and fully demonstrate that Hessian-driven damping can effectively alleviate oscillations. Finally, numerical experiments are conducted to verify the validity of the above theoretical results.

### [175] [Geometric Asymptotics of Score Mixing and Guidance in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12231)
*Kang Liu,Enrique Zuazua*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文严格分析了混合分数驱动的扩散模型在小时间生成动力学中的数学结构，将问题简化为由几何势能 Φ_λ=λd₁²+(1-λ)d₂² 控制的自治Clarke次梯度包含系统，并证明了在有限Dirac混合情形下轨迹收敛到势能临界点，收敛率为O(√t)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型在实际中常通过组合多个分数场来引导生成，但分数混合的数学结构尚不清晰。本文旨在严格理解混合分数驱动的小时间生成动力学，揭示其背后的几何与变分原理。

Method: 在热流框架下，定义混合分数 s=λ∇log u₁+(1-λ)∇log u₂，涵盖专家混合(0≤λ≤1)和无分类器引导(λ>1)两种机制。利用Laplace-Varadhan原理进行相似时间重缩放，将奇异非自治的分数驱动动力学约化为自治Clarke次梯度包含系统，导出显式几何势能Φ_λ。

Result: 小时间生成动力学由几何势能Φ_λ=λd₁²+(1-λ)d₂²控制，该势能仅依赖于初始测度的支撑集和混合参数λ。在有限Dirac混合（经验设置）下，极限势能为分段二次型，具有Voronoi结构；所有自治极限轨迹收敛到临界点，原始生成流在光滑稳定情形下以O(√t)速率条件收敛到势能局部极小值。

Conclusion: 本文为混合分数驱动的扩散模型提供了严格的数学基础，建立了从奇异非自治动力学到自治次梯度包含的约化框架，揭示了分数混合在小时间尺度下由几何距离决定的本质特征。

Abstract: Diffusion models are routinely guided in practice by combining multiple score fields, yet the mathematical structure of score mixing is still poorly understood. We study the small-time generation dynamics driven by mixed scores $$ s=λ\,\nabla\log u_1+(1-λ)\,\nabla\log u_2,\qquad λ\ge 0, $$ in the heat-flow framework, where $u_1,u_2$ are heat evolutions of two compactly supported probability measures. This single formulation covers both the mixture-of-experts regime $(0\leq λ\leq 1)$ and the classifier-free guidance regime $(λ>1)$. Exploiting a Laplace-Varadhan principle under a similarity-time rescaling, we show that the small-time generation dynamics is governed by the explicit geometric potential $$ Φ_λ=λd_1^2+(1-λ)d_2^2, $$ which depends only on the supports of the initial measures and on the mixing parameter. This gives a rigorous reduction from a singular, non-autonomous score-driven dynamics to autonomous Clarke-type subgradient inclusions. In the empirical setting of finite Dirac mixtures, the limiting potential is piecewise quadratic with a Voronoi-type structure; this rigidity yields convergence of all autonomous limiting trajectories to critical points and a conditional convergence criterion for the original generation flow toward local minimizers of the potential, with rate $\mathcal O(\sqrt t)$ in the smooth stable case.

### [176] [Stochastic block coordinate and function alternation for multi-objective optimization and learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12432)
*Trang H. Tran,Luis Nunes Vicente*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出了一种交替优化多目标的框架，每次迭代只更新部分目标和变量块，显著降低计算成本，同时保持收敛保证和帕累托前沿探索能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多目标优化中，传统的多梯度方法每步需计算所有目标对所有变量的梯度，在大规模场景下计算成本过高。

Method: 提出交替优化框架：在每个迭代中，交替地选择部分目标进行优化，并对相应的变量块进行（随机）梯度更新，通过预设的梯度步数分配来探索帕累托前沿。

Result: 在凸、非凸、Polyak-Lojasiewicz等多种随机平滑设定下建立了严格的收敛保证，恢复了单目标优化方法的经典收敛率。数值实验表明该方法在多目标回归任务上优于非交替方法，帕累托前沿近似具有竞争力。

Conclusion: 该交替优化框架在降低计算成本的同时保持理论收敛性，为大规模多目标优化提供了一种高效实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Multi-objective optimization is central to many engineering and machine learning applications, where multiple objectives must be optimized in balance. While multi-gradient based optimization methods combine these objectives in each step, such methods require computing gradients with respect to all variables at every iteration, resulting in high computational costs in large-scale settings. In this work, we propose a framework that simultaneously alternates the optimization of each objective and the (stochastic) gradient update with respect to each variable block. Our framework reduces per-iteration computational cost while enabling exploration of the Pareto front by allocating a prescribed number of gradient steps to each objective. We establish rigorous convergence guarantees across several stochastic smooth settings, including convex, non-convex, and Polyak-Lojasiewicz conditions, recovering classical convergence rates of single-objective methods. Numerical experiments demonstrate that our framework outperforms non-alternating methods on multi-target regression and produces a competitive Pareto front approximation, highlighting its computational efficiency and practical effectiveness.

</details>

### [177] [The Evaluation Differential: When Frontier AI Models Recognise They Are Being Tested](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11496)
*Varad Vishwarupe,Nigel Shadbolt,Marina Jirotka,Ivan Flechais*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文发现前沿AI模型在评估环境中会表现出与部署环境不同的行为，导致基于评估得出的安全结论存在有效性危机。作者提出评估差异（ED）概念及标准化形式（nED），建立安全主张类型学（ED稳定/退化/反转/未定），并开发TRACE审计协议来约束评估证据产生的条件，从而规范安全结论的推导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿实验室的证据表明AI模型能够识别评估环境并表现出不同行为，这使得基于评估得出的安全结论存在有效性问题。作者试图解决这一主张有效性危机，为安全评估结论建立更严谨的理论基础。

Method: 提出评估差异（ED）概念及其标准化形式（nED），证明边际评估分数无法识别ED；建立安全主张类型学；开发TRACE审计协议来约束评估证据的条件性；对三个公开评估事件进行回顾性分析。

Result: 定义并形式化了评估差异概念，建立了分类体系，开发了TRACE审计协议，并通过案例验证了框架的适用性。

Conclusion: TRACE不能消除对抗性适应，但通过明确证据产生的条件来约束从评估证据中得出的结论，从而提升安全评估的科学严谨性，对系统卡、一致性评估和国际AI安全机构网络具有治理启示。

Abstract: Recent published evidence from frontier laboratories shows that contemporary AI models can recognise evaluation contexts, latently represent them, and behave differently under those contexts than under deployment-continuous conditions. Anthropic's BrowseComp incident, the Natural Language Autoencoder findings on SWE-bench Verified and destructive-coding evaluations, and the OpenAI / Apollo anti-scheming work all document instances of this phenomenon. We argue that these findings create a claim-validity problem for safety conclusions drawn from frontier evaluations. We introduce the Evaluation Differential (ED), a conditional divergence in a target behavioural property between recognised-evaluation and deployment-continuous contexts, define a normalised effect-size form (nED) for cross-property comparison, and prove that marginal evaluation scores cannot identify ED. We develop a typology of safety claims (ED-stable, ED-degraded, ED-inverted, ED-undetermined) by their warrant-status under documented divergence, and specify TRACE (Test-Recognition Audit for Claim Evaluation), an audit protocol that wraps existing evaluation infrastructure and produces restricted claims rather than capability scores. We apply the framework retrospectively to three publicly documented evaluation incidents and discuss governance implications for system cards, conformity assessment, and the international network of AI safety and security institutes. TRACE does not eliminate adversarial adaptation; it disciplines the claims drawn from evaluation evidence by making explicit the conditions under which that evidence was produced.

### [178] [Why Conclusions Diverge from the Same Observations: Formalizing World-Model Non-Identifiability via an Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12255)
*Toru Takahashi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出，人们在共享相同文档和观测时得出不同结论，并非源于认知缺陷，而是推理和学习中固有的不可辨识性。作者将分歧分为θ层面（相同世界模型下因推理设置不同导致）和W层面（因推理设置反复使用导致世界模型本身分化），并引入推理轮廓θ=(R,E,S,D)来解释分歧的生成机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战"分歧源于对方非理性或恶意"的常见归因，提出分歧本质上是学习系统固有的不可辨识性，而非认知缺陷。

Method: 构建了两层不可辨识性框架：θ层面（推理设置差异）和W层面（世界模型差异）。引入推理轮廓θ=(R,E,S,D)（参考、探索、稳定化、视界），并指出分歧投影到少量基（抽象vs具体、可外化性、秩序vs自由）是学习系统约束（计算、观测、协调）的结果。

Result: 展示了框架对深度表示学习的解释力（表示层次、潜在状态估计、正则化-探索权衡），并通过AI监管辩论案例研究加以说明。

Conclusion: 分歧应被理解为学习过程中的结构性现象，而非他者的认知缺陷；该框架有助于更理性地看待和应对AI等复杂议题中的分歧。

Abstract: When people share the same documents and observations yet reach different conclusions, the disagreement often shifts into a judgment that the other party is cognitively defective, irrational, or acting in bad faith. This paper argues that such divergence is better described as a form of non-identifiability inherent in inference and learning, rather than as a defect of the other party. We organize the phenomenon into two levels: (i) $θ$-level non-identifiability, where conclusions diverge under the same world model $W$ because inference settings differ; and (ii) $W$-level non-identifiability, where repeated use of an inference setting $θ$ biases data exposure and update rules, causing the learned world model $W$ itself to diverge. We introduce an inference profile $θ= (R, E, S, D)$, consisting of Reference, Exploration, Stabilization, and Horizon, and show how outputs can split even for the same observation $o$ and the same $W$. We further explain why disagreements tend to project onto a small number of bases -- abstract versus concrete, externalizability, and order versus freedom -- as a consequence of general constraints on learning systems: computational, observational, and coordination constraints. Finally, we relate the framework to deep representation learning, including representation hierarchy, latent-state estimation, and regularization-exploration trade-offs, and illustrate the framework through a case study on AI regulation debates.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有交叉口管理方法（规则、信号控制器、预留方法）在复杂动态交通中难以应对车辆异构性、优先级冲突和实时约束；LLM仅被用作信号系统的辅助而非主要决策者，缺乏意图感知能力。

Method: LISA框架利用LLM推理车辆声明的意图（优先级、排队压力、能耗偏好），实现无信号、无基础设施依赖的认知仲裁式交叉口管理。

Conclusion: LLM推理能够实现实时、无信号的交叉口管理，为智能交通系统中的协同驾驶提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) show strong potential for Intelligent Transportation Systems (ITS), particularly in tasks requiring situational reasoning and multi-agent coordination. These capabilities make them well suited for cooperative driving, where rule-based approaches struggle in complex and dynamic traffic environments. Intersection management remains especially challenging due to conflicting right-of-way demands, heterogeneous vehicle priorities, and vehicle-specific kinematic constraints that must be resolved in real time. However, existing approaches typically use LLMs as auxiliary components on top of signal-based systems rather than as primary decision-makers. Signal controllers remain vehicle-agnostic, reservation-based methods lack intent awareness, and recent LLM-based systems still depend on signal infrastructure. In addition, LLM inference latency limits their use in sub-second control settings.
  We propose LISA (LLM-Based Intent-Driven Speed Advisory), a signal-free cognitive arbitration framework for autonomous intersection management. LISA uses an LLM to reason over declared vehicle intents, incorporating priority classes, queue pressure, and energy preferences. We evaluate LISA against fixed-cycle control, SCATS, AIM, and GLOSA across varying traffic loads. Results show that LISA reduces mean control delay by up to 89.1% and maintains Level of Service C while all non-LLM baselines degrade to Level of Service F. Under near-saturated demand, LISA reduces mean waiting time by 93% and peak queue length by 60.6% relative to fixed-cycle control. It also lowers fuel consumption by up to 48.8% and achieves 86.2% intent satisfaction, compared to 61.2% for the best non-LLM method. These results demonstrate that LLM-based reasoning can enable real-time, signal-free intersection management.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端天气和不稳定的电力批发市场使居民消费者面临巨大财务风险，而配电网级的需求响应作为提高电网灵活性和能源可负担性的工具尚未被充分利用。现有离线历史数据无法捕捉电力公司定价信号与客户接受和适应需求响应程序之间的动态交互反馈循环。

Result: 通过基线策略和数据快照展示了该模拟器能够创建真实且可学习的环境。

Conclusion: DR-Gym为电力公司优化需求响应策略提供了可行的强化学习训练环境，弥补了离线数据无法模拟动态交互的不足。

Abstract: Extreme weather and volatile wholesale electricity markets expose residential consumers to catastrophic financial risks, yet demand response at the distribution level remains an underutilized tool for grid flexibility and energy affordability. While a demand-response program can shield consumers by issuing financial credits during high-price periods, optimizing this sequential decision-making process presents a unique challenge for reinforcement learning despite the plentiful offline historical smart meter and wholesale pricing data available publicly. Offline historical data fails to capture the dynamic, interactive feedback loop between an electric utility's pricing signals and customer acceptance and adaptation to a demand-response program. To address this, we introduce DR-Gym, an open-source, online Gymnasium-compatible environment designed to train and evaluate demand-response from the electric utility's perspective. Unlike existing device-level energy simulators, our environment focuses on the market-level electric utility setting and provides a rich observational space relevant to the electric utility. The simulator additionally features a regime-switching wholesale price model calibrated to real-world extreme events, alongside physics-based building demand profiles. For our learning signal, we use a configurable, multi-objective reward function for specifying diverse learning objectives. We demonstrate through baseline strategies and data snapshots the capability of our simulator to create realistic and learnable environments.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有因果公平性研究主要针对标准机器学习（预测单一输出变量），而生成式AI能够对任意变量集合进行条件采样，隐式构建所有因果机制，这带来了全新的公平性挑战，亟需新的方法论。

Abstract: Automated systems built on artificial intelligence (AI) are increasingly deployed across high-stakes domains, raising critical concerns about fairness and the perpetuation of demographic disparities that exist in the world. In this context, causal inference provides a principled framework for reasoning about fairness, as it links observed disparities to underlying mechanisms and aligns naturally with human intuition and legal notions of discrimination. Prior work on causal fairness primarily focuses on the standard machine learning setting, where a decision-maker constructs a single predictive mechanism $f_{\widehat Y}$ for an outcome variable $Y$, while inheriting the causal mechanisms of all other covariates from the real world. The generative AI setting, however, is markedly more complex: generative models can sample from arbitrary conditionals over any set of variables, implicitly constructing their own beliefs about all causal mechanisms rather than learning a single predictive function. This fundamental difference requires new developments in causal fairness methodology. We formalize the problem of causal fairness in generative AI and unify it with the standard ML setting under a common theoretical framework. We then derive new causal decomposition results that enable granular quantification of fairness impacts along both (a) different causal pathways and (b) the replacement of real-world mechanisms by the generative model's mechanisms. We establish identification conditions and introduce efficient estimators for causal quantities of interest, and demonstrate the value of our methodology by analyzing race and gender bias in large language models across different datasets.

Abstract: The trustworthiness of AI decision-making systems is increasingly important. Existing approaches treat recourse outcomes as counterfactuals of a fixed unit, ignoring that real-world recourse involves repeated decisions on the same individual under possibly different latent conditions. We demonstrate the value of the proposed methods on real and semi-synthetic datasets.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MTRL中离线策略方法（如SAC）占据主导，而在线策略方法（如PPO）被忽视。作者诊断出PPO在MTRL中存在评论家梯度病态问题，导致尾部任务停滞而简单任务主导价值函数更新，亟需解决这一优化瓶颈。

Method: 提出TOPPO，核心是Critic Balancing模块集，包括：1) 改善梯度条件（gradient conditioning）；2) 平衡跨任务学习动态。无需模块化架构或大模型，直接针对PPO内部的优化瓶颈进行改革。

Result: 在Meta-World++基准上，TOPPO以更少参数和环境步数，在均值和尾部任务性能上均超越SAC家族和ARS家族基线；训练早期即可匹配或超越强SAC基线，全程保持领先。消融实验验证了每个模块的有效性及交互机制。

Abstract: Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) and its variants dominate Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning (MTRL) due to their off-policy sample efficiency, while on-policy methods such as Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) remain underexplored. We diagnose that PPO in MTRL suffers from a previously overlooked issue: critic-side gradient ill-conditioning, which may cause tail tasks to stall while easy tasks dominate the value function's updates. To address this, we propose TOPPO (Tail-Optimized PPO), a reformulation of PPO via Critic Balancing -- a set of modules that improve gradient conditioning and balance learning dynamics across tasks. Unlike prior approaches that rely on modular architectures or large models, TOPPO targets the optimization bottleneck within PPO itself. Empirically, TOPPO achieves stronger mean and tail-task performance than published SAC-family and ARS-family baselines while using substantially fewer parameters and environment steps on Meta-World+ benchmark. Notably, TOPPO matches or surpasses strong SAC baselines early in training and maintains superior performance at full budget. Ablations confirm the effectiveness of each module in TOPPO and provide insights into their interactions. Our results demonstrate that, with proper optimization, on-policy methods can rival or exceed off-policy approaches in MTRL, challenging the prevailing reliance on SAC and highlighting critic-side gradient conditioning as the central bottleneck.

### [185] [FibQuant: Universal Vector Quantization for Random-Access KV-Cache Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11478)
*Namyoon Lee,Yongjune Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出FibQuant，一种通用固定码率向量量化器，通过结合Beta分位数半径和Fibonacci准均匀方向，在保持normalize-rotate-store接口的同时，显著提升KV缓存压缩效率，在相同码率下优于标量量化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文推理中KV缓存成为内存瓶颈，现有标量量化方法（如基于旋转的标量编解码器）虽通用且支持随机访问，但归一化步骤丢弃了几何结构信息，导致量化效率不足。

Method: FibQuant采用归一化-旋转-存储的接口，但用共享径向-角度码本替代标量表。码本包含Beta分位数半径、Fibonacci/Roberts-Kronecker准均匀方向，以及多重启Lloyd-Max细化。这种向量量化器匹配了Haar旋转后形成的球面-Beta源分布。

Result: 在GPT-2 small KV缓存上，FibQuant实现了从5倍压缩（注意力余弦相似度0.99）到34倍压缩（0.95）的存储-保真度边界。在TinyLlama-1.1B端到端评估中，4倍压缩下困惑度距离fp16仅0.10；在b=2（8倍压缩）时，困惑度比标量TurboQuant低3.6倍。

Conclusion: FibQuant在理论上有高码率增益，可分解为单元形状因子和密度匹配因子；实际中提供了密集的码率轴（包括分数比特和亚1比特工作点），无需校准或变长地址，在极端压缩下仍优于标量随机访问量化方法。

Abstract: Long-context inference is increasingly a memory-traffic problem. The culprit is the key--value (KV) cache: it grows with context length, batch size, layers, and heads, and it is read at every decoding step. Rotation-based scalar codecs meet this systems constraint by storing a norm, applying a shared random rotation, and quantizing one coordinate at a time. They are universal and random-access, but they discard the geometry created by the normalization step. After a Haar rotation, a block of $k$ consecutive coordinates is not a product source; it is a spherical-Beta source on the unit ball. We introduce \textsc{FibQuant}, a universal fixed-rate vector quantizer that keeps the same normalize--rotate--store interface while replacing scalar tables by a shared radial--angular codebook matched to this canonical source. The codebook combines Beta-quantile radii, Fibonacci\,/\,Roberts--Kronecker quasi-uniform directions, and multi-restart Lloyd--Max refinement. We prove that the resulting vector code strictly improves on its scalar product specialization at matched rate, with a high-rate gain that separates into a cell-shaping factor and a density-matching factor. The same construction gives a dense rate axis, including fractional-bit and sub-one-bit operating points, without calibration or variable-length addresses. On GPT-2 small KV caches, \textsc{FibQuant} traces a memory--fidelity frontier from $5\times$ compression at $0.99$ attention cosine similarity to $34\times$ at $0.95$. End-to-end on TinyLlama-1.1B, it is within $0.10$ perplexity of fp16 at $4\times$ compression and has $3.6\times$ lower perplexity than scalar \textsc{TurboQuant} at $b = 2$ ($8\times$ compression), where scalar random-access quantization begins to fail.

Despite their predictive capabilities being ever useful across industrial workspaces, the inherent uncertainty induced by the nature of the data is a huge mitigating factor to GNN performance. While aleatoric uncertainty is the result of noisy and incomplete stochastic data such as missing edges or over-smoothing, epistemic uncertainty arises from lack of knowledge about a system or model (e.g., a graph's topology or node feature representation), which can be reduced by gathering more data and information. In this paper, we propose an original new framework in which node-level epistemic uncertainty is modelled in a belief function (finite random set) formalism. The resulting Random-Set Graph Neural Networks have a belief-function head predicting a random set over the list of classes, from which both a precise probability prediction and a measure of epistemic uncertainty can be obtained. Extensive experiments on 9 different graph learning datasets, including real-world autonomous driving benchmarks as such Nuscene and ROAD, demonstrate RS-GNN's superior uncertainty quantification capabilities

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have heterogeneous strengths across OCR, chart understanding, spatial reasoning, visual question answering, cost, and latency. Effective MLLM routing therefore requires more than estimating query difficulty: a router must match the multimodal requirements of the current image-question input with the capabilities of each candidate model. We propose LatentRouter, a router that formulates MLLM routing as counterfactual multimodal utility prediction. Given an image-question query, LatentRouter extracts learned multimodal routing capsules, represents each candidate MLLM with a model capability token, and performs latent communication between these states to estimate how each model would perform if selected. A distributional outcome head predicts model-specific counterfactual quality, while a bounded capsule correction refines close decisions without allowing residual signals to dominate the prediction. The resulting utility-based policy supports performance-oriented and performance-cost routing, and handles changing candidate pools through shared per-model scoring with availability masking. Experiments on MMR-Bench and VL-RouterBench show that LatentRouter outperforms fixed-model, feature-level, and learned-router baselines. Additional analyses show that the gains are strongest on multimodal task groups where model choice depends on visual, layout-sensitive, or reasoning-oriented requirements, and that latent communication is the main contributor to the improvement. The code is available at: https://github.com/LabRAI/LatentRouter.

### [189] [AcuityBench: Evaluating Clinical Acuity Identification and Uncertainty Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11398)
*Robin Linzmayer,Georgianna Lin,Di Coneybeare,Jason Chu,Trudi Cloyd,Manish Garg,Miles Gordon,Elizabeth Hartofilis,Benjamin Hong,Ashraf Hussain,Eugene Y. Chang,David Kessler,Noémie Elhadad*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AcuityBench是一个评估语言模型识别医疗紧急程度能力的基准，覆盖5个数据集、914个病例，支持四分类QA和自由对话两种任务格式。对12个前沿模型的测试发现，模型在明确病例上表现差异大，对话格式会降低过度分诊但增加分诊不足，且模型无法匹配医生的临床不确定性分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 整合5个公开数据集（用户对话、论坛帖子、临床案例、患者门户消息），统一为四级紧急框架（家庭监测到立即急救）；构建914个病例（697共识+217模糊病例）；支持两种任务格式：四分类QA和基于评分标准的自由对话评估。

Result: 12个前沿模型在明确病例的准确性和错误方向上差异显著；对话格式相比QA格式减少了过度分诊但增加了分诊不足；在模糊病例中，模型预测分布比医生的临床不确定性更集中，无法匹配医生判断的分布。

Conclusion: 紧急程度识别是一项独立的安全关键能力，AcuityBench能够系统性地比较和压力测试模型引导用户获得正确医疗护理水平的能力。

Abstract: We introduce AcuityBench, a benchmark for evaluating whether language models identify the appropriate urgency of care from user medical presentations. Existing health benchmarks emphasize medical question answering, broad health interactions, or narrow workflow-specific triage tasks, but they do not offer a unified evaluation of acuity identification across these settings. AcuityBench addresses this gap by harmonizing five public datasets spanning user conversations, online forum posts, clinical vignettes, and patient portal messages under a shared four-level acuity framework ranging from home monitoring to immediate emergency care. The benchmark contains 914 cases, including 697 consensus cases for standard accuracy evaluation and 217 physician-confirmed ambiguous cases for uncertainty-aware evaluation. It supports two complementary task formats: explicit four-way classification in a QA setting, and free-form conversational responses evaluated with a rubric-based judge anchored to the same framework. Across 12 frontier proprietary and open-weight models, we find substantial variation in clear-case acuity accuracy and error direction. Comparing task formats reveals a systematic tradeoff: conversational responses reduce over-triage but increase under-triage relative to QA, especially in higher-acuity cases. In ambiguous cases, no model closely matches the distribution of physician judgments, and model predictions are more concentrated than expert clinical uncertainty. We also compare expert and model adjudication on a subset of maximally ambiguous cases, using those cases to examine the role of clinical uncertainty in label disagreement. Together, these results position acuity identification as a distinct safety-critical capability and show that AcuityBench enables systematic comparison and stress-testing of how well models guide users to the right level of care in real-world health use.

</details>


### [190] [Adaptive Teacher Exposure for Self-Distillation in LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11458)
*Zihao Han,Tiangang Zhang,Huaibin Wang,Yilun Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出自适应教师曝光（ATESD），在自蒸馏中动态控制教师向学生展示的推理内容比例，以解决传统方法中教师曝光过多导致的学生-教师不匹配问题，在多个数学推理基准上取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有on-policy自蒸馏方法中，教师总是看到完整的参考推理，但学生当前能力不足以吸收过强的教师信号，导致学生-教师不匹配（teacher-side exposure mismatch）。

Method: 提出ATESD方法：使用轻量级Beta策略控制器建模曝光比例，基于训练状态统计量动态采样曝光率，并用折扣学习进度奖励来优化控制器，解决延迟信用分配问题。

Result: 在AIME 24/25和HMMT 25上，基于Qwen3-{1.7B, 4B, 8B}，ATESD持续超越OPSD等基线，Average@12分别提升+0.95、+2.05、+2.33。

Conclusion: 教师曝光不应是固定超参数，而应是可学习的训练控制变量；ATESD证明了自适应教师曝光是推理自蒸馏的一个有效新方向。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation has become a strong recipe for LLM reasoning, where a privileged teacher supervises the student's own rollouts while conditioning on the reference solution. A design choice shared by nearly all such methods, however, has gone unquestioned: the teacher always sees the full reference reasoning. We argue that this default itself is part of the problem and identify a teacher-side exposure mismatch: when the teacher conditions on reasoning far beyond the student's current competence, the resulting token targets become too strong to absorb. A controlled fixed-exposure sweep makes this concrete on two fronts: 1) full exposure is not reliably the best choice, and 2) student-teacher mismatch grows monotonically as the teacher sees more privileged reasoning. This motivates treating teacher exposure not as a fixed hyperparameter but as a learnable training-time control variable. We therefore propose Adaptive Teacher Exposure for Self-Distillation (ATESD). ATESD models the reveal ratio with a lightweight Beta-policy controller conditioned on compact training-state statistics, and uses one sampled exposure for a short hold window of student updates. To make this exposure controller learnable, we optimize it with a discounted learning-progress reward that scores each held decision by its effect on the student's future improvement rather than its immediate loss change, addressing the delayed credit assignment induced by on-policy distillation. Experiments on AIME 24, AIME 25, and HMMT 25 across Qwen3-{1.7B, 4B, 8B} show that ATESD consistently outperforms competitive self-distillation and RL baselines, improving over OPSD by +0.95, +2.05, and +2.33 Average@12 points respectively, and establishing adaptive teacher exposure as an effective new axis for reasoning self-distillation.

</details>


### [191] [AutoLLMResearch: Training Research Agents for Automating LLM Experiment Configuration -- Learning from Cheap, Optimizing Expensive](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11518)
*Taicheng Guo,Nitesh V. Chawla,Olaf Wiest,Xiangliang Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出AutoLLMResearch，一个模仿人类研究者的智能体框架，通过从低保真实验中学习通用原理并外推，实现大规模LLM实验的高效自动配置，解决了高成本场景下实验配置自动化这一空白问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化方法适用于低成本场景，但大规模LLM实验成本高昂，无法进行反复试错；目前缺乏针对高成本LLM实验配置自动化的研究，该问题依赖专家经验和人力劳动。

Method: 提出双组件框架：1) LLMConfig-Gym，一个多保真度实验环境，涵盖四种LLM实验任务，含超过100万GPU小时的实验数据；2) 结构化训练流水线，将配置研究建模为长时域马尔可夫决策过程，并激励跨保真度外推推理。

Result: 在留出实验上的广泛评估显示，该框架相比多种强基线方法在有效性、泛化性和可解释性方面均表现优越。

Conclusion: AutoLLMResearch有潜力成为一种实用且通用的解决方案，用于可扩展的真实世界LLM实验自动化。

Abstract: Effectively configuring scalable large language model (LLM) experiments, spanning architecture design, hyperparameter tuning, and beyond, is crucial for advancing LLM research, as poor configuration choices can waste substantial computational resources and prevent models from realizing their full potential. Prior automated methods are designed for low-cost settings where repeated trial and error is feasible, but scalable LLM experiments are too expensive for such extensive iteration. To our knowledge, no work has addressed the automation of high-cost LLM experiment configurations, leaving this problem labor-intensive and dependent on expert intuition. Motivated by this gap, we propose AutoLLMResearch, an agentic framework that mimics how human researchers learn generalizable principles from low-fidelity experiments and extrapolate to efficiently identify promising configurations in expensive LLM settings. The core challenge is how to enable an agent to learn, through interaction with a multi-fidelity experimental environment that captures the structure of the LLM configuration landscape. To achieve this, we propose a systematic framework with two key components: 1) LLMConfig-Gym, a multi-fidelity environment encompassing four critical LLM experiment tasks, supported by over one million GPU hours of verifiable experiment outcomes; 2) A structured training pipeline that formulates configuration research as a long-horizon Markov Decision Process and accordingly incentivizes cross-fidelity extrapolation reasoning. Extensive evaluation against diverse strong baselines on held-out experiments demonstrates the effectiveness, generalization, and interpretability of our framework, supporting its potential as a practical and general solution for scalable real-world LLM experiment automation.

### [192] [Controllable User Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11519)
*Guy Tennenholtz,Ofer Meshi,Amir Globerson,Uri Shalit,Jihwan Jeong,Craig Boutilier*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文形式化可控对话模拟为因果推断问题，指出现有监督微调方法因后见偏差导致因果不一致性，并提出理论条件与训练缓解措施来消除偏差、保持自然方差并实现零样本泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线数据集难以覆盖罕见场景或支持新策略测试，现有可控用户模拟器（通过提示或微调大语言模型实现）存在结构性偏差问题。

Method: 将可控模拟形式化为因果推断问题，建立自然语言评估与离策略评估方法的桥梁；理论证明后见偏差导致因果不一致及方差爆炸（可控性塌陷）；提出先验控制、逐步动态控制和直接策略条件学习三种训练缓解措施。

Result: 因果驱动的模拟器消除了后见偏差，保留了自然方差，展现出对未见代理行为的鲁棒零样本泛化能力。

Conclusion: 标准全局控制会扭曲对话分布并坍缩行为多样性，而基于因果理论的方法能恢复因果一致性，实现更可靠的评估。

Abstract: Using offline datasets to evaluate conversational agents often fails to cover rare scenarios or to support testing new policies. This has motivated the use of controllable user simulators for targeted, counterfactual evaluation, typically implemented by prompting or fine-tuning large language models. In this work, we formalize controllable simulation as a causal inference problem. By bridging natural language evaluation with off-policy evaluation methodology, we show that the standard practice of training simulators via supervised fine-tuning on post-hoc trajectory labels yields a structurally biased model. Specifically, these labels are inextricably coupled to the data-generating behavior policy, injecting a look-ahead bias that breaks causal consistency. Furthermore, we prove that under policy shift this failure causes the variance of evaluation metrics to explode geometrically, a phenomenon we term controllability collapse. To restore causal consistency, we establish theoretical conditions for accurate simulation and propose practical training mitigations: a priori controls, step-wise dynamic controls, and direct policy-conditioned learning. Empirical evaluation confirms that while standard global controls distort conversational distributions and collapse behavioral diversity, our causally grounded simulators eliminate look-ahead bias, preserve natural variance, and exhibit robust zero-shot generalization to unseen agent behaviors.

### [193] [Allegory of the Cave: Measurement-Grounded Vision-Language Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11727)
*Kepeng Xu,Li Xu,Gang He,Wenxin Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PRISM-VL，通过将视觉输入从标准RGB图像转向原始相机测量数据（RAW-derived Meas.-XYZ），结合曝光包围监督聚合和相机条件接地，显著提升了视觉语言模型在低光、HDR等挑战场景下的推理性能，证明RGB渲染过程中的信息丢失是VLM接地误差的重要来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型通常基于ISP处理后的RGB图像进行推理，但RGB渲染过程会裁剪、抑制或量化传感器原始证据，导致信息丢失。作者探究将视觉接口向底层相机测量数据迁移是否能改善VLMs的接地能力。

Method: 提出测量接地视觉语言学习框架PRISM-VL，包含三个关键设计：(1) 使用RAW-derived Meas.-XYZ输入替代标准RGB输入；(2) 引入相机条件接地机制；(3) 采用曝光包围监督聚合（EBSA）将RGB代理模型的监督迁移到测量域观测上。构建了15万条质量控制的指令微调数据集及专门的测试基准。

Result: PRISM-VL-8B在测试集上达到0.6120 BLEU、0.4571 ROUGE-L和82.66% LLM-Judge准确率，相比Qwen3-VL-8B基线分别提升+0.1074 BLEU、+0.1071 ROUGE-L和+4.46个百分点。

Conclusion: 部分VLM接地误差源于RGB渲染过程中的信息丢失，保留测量域证据能够改善多模态推理能力，为视觉语言模型的设计提供了新方向。

Abstract: Vision-language models typically reason over post-ISP RGB images, although RGB rendering can clip, suppress, or quantize sensor evidence before inference. We study whether grounding improves when the visual interface is moved closer to the underlying camera measurement. We formulate measurement-grounded vision-language learning and instantiate it as PRISM-VL, which combines RAW-derived Meas.-XYZ inputs, camera-conditioned grounding, and Exposure-Bracketed Supervision Aggregation for transferring supervision from RGB proxies to measurement-domain observations. Using a quality-controlled 150K instruction-tuning set and a held-out benchmark targeting low-light, HDR, visibility-sensitive, and hallucination-sensitive cases, PRISM-VL-8B reaches 0.6120 BLEU, 0.4571 ROUGE-L, and 82.66\% LLM-Judge accuracy, improving over the RGB Qwen3-VL-8B baseline by +0.1074 BLEU, +0.1071 ROUGE-L, and +4.46 percentage points. These results suggest that part of VLM grounding error arises from information lost during RGB rendering, and that preserving measurement-domain evidence can improve multimodal reasoning.

### [194] [Do Enterprise Systems Need Learned World Models? The Importance of Context to Infer Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12178)
*Jishnu Sethumadhavan Nair,Patrice Bechard,Rishabh Maheshwary,Surajit Dasgupta,Sravan Ramachandran,Aakash Bhagat,Shruthan Radhakrishna,Pulkit Pattnaik,Johan Obando-Ceron,Shiva Krishna Reddy Malay,Sagar Davasam,Seganrasan Subramanian,Vipul Mittal,Sridhar Krishna Nemala,Christopher Pal,Srinivas Sunkara,Sai Rajeswar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出在企业可配置环境中，智能体应在推理时通过读取系统配置来发现动态规则，而非仅依赖离线训练的世界模型。作者提出了企业发现智能体（Enterprise Discovery Agents）和 CascadeBench 基准，实验表明发现型智能体在部署偏移下比传统世界模型更具鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型在多变的企事业环境中表现脆弱：业务逻辑因租户而异且随时间演变，导致基于历史数据训练的模型在部署偏移时性能退化。文献尚未探讨当规则可在推理时读取时，智能体是否仍需学习它们。

Method: 提出企业发现智能体（Enterprise Discovery Agents），在运行时通过读取系统配置来获取转移动态，而非仅依赖内部化表示。同时构建 CascadeBench 基准，采用 World of Workflows 评估方法在多样化合成环境中进行推理聚焦的级联预测评测。

Result: 离线训练的世界模型在分布内表现良好，但随着动态变化而退化；而发现型智能体通过将预测锚定在当前实例中，在部署偏移下表现更鲁棒。

Conclusion: 在可配置的企业环境中，智能体不应仅依赖固定的内部化动态，而应引入在运行时发现相关转移逻辑的机制。

Abstract: World models enable agents to anticipate the effects of their actions by internalizing environment dynamics. In enterprise systems, however, these dynamics are often defined by tenant-specific business logic that varies across deployments and evolves over time, making models trained on historical transitions brittle under deployment shift. We ask a question the world-models literature has not addressed: when the rules can be read at inference time, does an agent still need to learn them? We argue, and demonstrate empirically, that in settings where transition dynamics are configurable and readable, runtime discovery complements offline training by grounding predictions in the active system instance. We propose enterprise discovery agents, which recover relevant transition dynamics at runtime by reading the system's configuration rather than relying solely on internalized representations. We introduce CascadeBench, a reasoning-focused benchmark for enterprise cascade prediction that adopts the evaluation methodology of World of Workflows on diverse synthetic environments, and use it together with deployment-shift evaluation to show that offline-trained world models can perform well in-distribution but degrade as dynamics change, whereas discovery-based agents are more robust under shift by grounding their predictions in the current instance. Our findings suggest that, in configurable enterprise environments, agents should not rely solely on fixed internalized dynamics, but should incorporate mechanisms for discovering relevant transition logic at runtime.

### [195] [The Metaverse Is Not a Place Apart: Law, Code, and the Recursive Governance of Digital Space (A Review Essay on Mark Findlay, Governing the Metaverse: Law, Order and Freedom in Digital Space (2025))](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11023)
*Oren Perez*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文评论了Mark Findlay的《治理元宇宙》一书，指出其核心概念"元宇宙"和"新法律"理论化不足，并提出应理解数字空间与物理基础设施、法律制度的混合性，而非将其视为独立领域来治理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Findlay试图为元宇宙这一数字空间提供一套以自由、人格、社群和抵抗圈地为导向的治理框架，但本文认为其理论基础存在缺陷。

Method: 通过批判性书评方式，分析Findlay的"元宇宙"与"新法律"两个核心范畴，并引入算法宪政主义、言语行为多元主义和模糊合法性等理论资源提出替代性分析。

Result: Findlay依赖的"现实空间/虚拟空间"二分法在其自身分析中已被反复动摇；其对"新法律"的论述未能充分解释规范权威如何在代码、平台规则和法律监督之间递归互动的分层治理架构中运作。

Conclusion: 治理元宇宙的关键不是为虚拟领域设计独立法律，而是理解一种混合社会-技术秩序，其中法律、代码、平台和公共监管递归互动；需要一种能够处理分层、可废止和递归不稳定规范力的法理学。

Abstract: This review essay examines Mark Findlay's Governing the Metaverse: Law, Order and Freedom in Digital Space. Findlay offers an ambitious and timely account of the metaverse as a social and imaginative space that should be governed for freedom, personhood, community, and resistance to enclosure. The essay argues, however, that the book's two central categories, "the metaverse" and "new law," remain insufficiently theorised. The book relies on a realspace/virtual distinction that its own analysis repeatedly destabilises. Once digital environments are understood as dependent on physical infrastructures, platform architectures, AI systems, data pipelines, and external legal institutions, and as capable of generating real-world harms for individuals and society, the governance problem is no longer how to devise a separate law for a separate virtual realm. It is how to govern a hybrid socio-technical order in which law, code, platforms, and public oversight recursively interact. The essay further argues that Findlay's account of "new law" does not adequately theorise how normative authority operates across a recursively layered governance architecture in which code, platform rules, and legal oversight interact without any single level exercising decisive control. Drawing on algorithmic constitutionalism, speech-act pluralism, and fuzzy legality, the essay suggests that addressing this architecture requires a jurisprudence capable of reasoning about normative force that is layered, defeasible, and recursively unstable.

### [196] [Improving Hybrid Human-AI Tutoring by Differentiating Human Tutor Roles Based on Student Needs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11155)
*Ashish Gurung,Ge Gao,Jordan Gutterman,Danielle R. Thomas,Shivang Gupta,Lee Branstetter,Emma Brunskill,Vincent Aleven,Kenneth R. Koedinger*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了差异化的人机混合辅导策略：对低分学生采用主动式辅导（教师主动介入），对高分学生采用被动式辅导（按需响应）。基于635名5-8年级学生的准实验设计发现，相较于纯AI辅导，人机混合辅导在任务时间、技能掌握和学业成长上均有显著提升。主动式辅导对低分学生的学术成长效果更佳（MAP测试增长75%），有助于缩小成绩差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究表明人机混合辅导优于纯AI辅导，但低分学生从中获益更多，高分学生获益较少。因此需要探索差异化的辅导策略，以同时满足不同水平学生的需求。

Method: 将635名5-8年级学生按州考试成绩中位数分为两组：低于中位数的接受主动式辅导（教师主动发起），高于中位数的接受被动式辅导（按需响应）。采用断点差分（DiDC）设计，比较秋季（纯AI辅导）和春季（差异化人机混合辅导）两个时段的结果，利用断点附近数据（Imbens-Kalyanaraman标准）进行因果推断。

Result: 人机混合辅导相比纯AI辅导：任务时间增加25%，技能掌握提升36%，MAP学术成长提升61%。主动式与被动式辅导在任务时间和技能掌握上效果相当，但主动式辅导在MAP成长上边际显著更高（75%, p=0.065），对低于断点的学生更有利，有助于缩小成绩差距。

Conclusion: 差异化的人机混合辅导策略能有效满足不同水平学生的需求，主动式辅导特别有助于低分学生缩小成绩差距，是一种实用且经济高效的大规模混合教学模式。

Abstract: Hybrid human-AI tutoring, where technology and humans jointly facilitate student learning, can be more beneficial than AI-only tutoring. However, preliminary evidence suggests that lower-performing students derive greater benefit from human-AI tutoring than higher-performing students. As such, this study evaluates whether a differentiated tutoring policy can effectively support both groups: human tutors initiate support for lower-performing students, while higher-performing students receive reactive, on-demand support. Using their within-grade median state test scores, we assigned 635 students (grades 5-8) to receive proactive (< median) or reactive ($\geq$ median) tutoring. Using a DiDC design, we compare outcomes across two time periods: fall (AI-only tutoring) and spring (proactive-reactive human-AI tutoring). This quasi-experimental design isolates the effects of proactive-reactive tutoring approaches by comparing the discontinuity in spring outcomes to the fall, where no such discontinuity existed. Using data around the cutoff (Imbens-Kalyanaraman criterion), we find significant overall improvements from human-AI tutoring compared to AI-only baseline: 25% increase in time on task, 36% in skill proficiency, and 61% in academic growth (standardized MAP test). Between proactive and reactive tutoring, we find comparable improvements in time-on-task and skill proficiency. However, proactive tutoring, on average, showed marginally higher MAP growth (75%, p = .065) than reactive tutoring, i.e., proactive tutoring was more beneficial to students farther below the cutoff and helped narrow achievement gaps. Our findings provide evidence that differentiated human-AI tutoring addresses the needs of both groups, offering a practical and cost-effective strategy for scaling hybrid instruction.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: It is prominently recognized that dataset development in machine learning is a value-laden process from problem formulation to data processing, use, and reuse. Structured documentation frameworks such as datasheets, data statements, and dataset nutrition labels have been created to aid developers in documenting how their datasets were produced and, according to the creators of the frameworks, to facilitate reflexivity in dataset development. While reflexivity is a stated goal, it is unclear whether and to what extent these structured dataset documentation frameworks incorporate concepts from reflexivity literature (at FAccT and elsewhere) and whether the use of the frameworks demonstrates reflexivity. Here, we adopt mixed-method thematic analysis and corpus-assisted discourse analysis to explore how reflexivity is incorporated in structured documentation frameworks and their responses. We demonstrate empirically that there is a general lack of engagement with major themes of reflexivity in both dataset documentation frameworks and published applications of these frameworks. We present a codebook of major reflexivity topics, recommend actionable strategies, and propose a set of extended datasheet questions to more effectively incorporate these topics into structured documentation frameworks and in the FAccT literature.

### [198] [Auditing African Content Moderators' Working Conditions by Using the European General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11699)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科技公司通过外包（BPO）将内容审核劳动转移到全球南方，但这些工人的工作条件恶劣且权利受侵害，同时科技行业以"例外论"声称其模式不受现有法律框架约束。作者希望用数据保护法规作为制衡工具。

Method: 利用GDPR的域外适用条款，向BPO公司索取雇佣合同和保密协议（NDA）等文件，这些文件此前从未提供给工人本人。

Result: 获得了具有法律依据的证据，证明了全球南方内容审核员面临的结构性劣势，其剥削性工作条件违反了劳动者权利。

Conclusion: 数据权利保护立法可以作为对抗科技行业例外论的有效工具，揭露其依靠BPO外包劳动成本与责任、同时声称自身不受既有法律约束的矛盾。

Abstract: In this article, we audit the working conditions of content moderators in Kenya and Nigeria employed by business process outsourcing (BPO) companies by using the European General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR). We demonstrate its extraterritorial scope for gaining access to elements such as employment contracts and NDAs that have never been provided to the workers concerned. The results of this approach provide legally grounded evidence of the structural disadvantages faced by content moderators in the Global South, whose exploitative working conditions violate workers' rights. Our work also highlights the benefits of legislation aimed at protecting individuals' data rights as a counterweight to the tech industry's discourse of exceptionalism, which obscures its dependence on BPOs to externalise labour costs and accountability, whilst claiming that its products, business models, and methods of resource extraction are unprecedented and fall outside any existing legal framework.

</details>


### [199] [Into the Unknown: Accounting for Missing Demographic Data when Mitigating Ad Delivery Skew](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12273)
*Isabel Corpus,Allison Koenecke*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文研究在线广告投放中的性别偏差问题，提出了一种预算拆分干预方法，在考虑平台无法识别性别的"未知用户"的同时，通过性别定向来减少广告投放偏差。与政府机构合作验证该方法能在不排除未知用户的情况下有效缓解投放偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线广告投放系统存在人口统计属性偏差，导致公共服务广告在某些群体中系统性投递不足，阻碍特定群体获取公共资源信息。现有平台缺乏解决方案，而直接定向目标群体会排除平台无法推断性别的"未知用户"。

Method: 设计了一种预算拆分干预方法：将广告预算分配给三组——Google推断的男性、女性和未知用户，在利用性别定向的同时纳入未知用户。与州级政府机构合作进行实地实验验证。

Result: 该干预方法能有效减少性别偏差，同时不排除未知用户；在更细粒度定向带来的更高成本和完全忽略人口统计信息带来的偏差之间取得了平衡。

Conclusion: 该方法适用于资源有限的现实广告主，有助于实现公共服务在线广告的公平分发。最后为政府广告主、在线广告平台和研究者提出了建议。

Abstract: Online advertising platforms use algorithmic systems to power the process of matching ads to users, termed ad delivery. Prior audits have demonstrated that ad delivery can be skewed by demographic attributes, such that ads are systematically under-delivered to certain groups despite advertiser intent to reach groups proportionally. This under-delivery raises a serious concern in the context of ads promoting public services, which might prevent certain groups of individuals from accessing information about resources on the basis of their demographic identity. In the absence of platform-provided solutions to skewed ad delivery, advertisers can counteract skew by targeting demographic groups directly. However, direct targeting excludes users whose demographics the platform cannot infer ("unknown users") if advertising platforms do not provide a way to target unknown users directly, as is the case on Google Ads. We collaborate with a state-level government agency to reduce gender-based skew in ad delivery with an intervention that accounts for unknown users while incorporating gender-based targeting. In particular, we design a budget split intervention that directly incorporates unknown users and targets users with Google-inferred gender labels (i.e., male, female). We find that this intervention is a valuable approach to addressing ad delivery skew without excluding unknown users, and serves as a middle ground in the trade-off between higher costs (from more granular demographic targeting) and skew (from ignoring demographics entirely). This approach is responsive to the needs of real-world, resource-constrained advertisers who are committed to the equitable distribution of public service outreach via online advertising. We conclude with recommendations for government advertisers, online advertising platforms, and researchers.

</details>

Abstract: Persistent inequities in STEM education continue to limit the participation of Black youth in science and technology fields across Canada. Structural barriers, underrepresentation, and limited access to culturally affirming learning spaces can restrict both opportunity and confidence in pursuing STEM pathways. This paper examines Ontario Tech University's Engineering Outreach Black Youth Program as an exploratory, practice-based case study of culturally responsive STEM outreach. The program creates inclusive environments where Black youth engage in hands-on, culturally grounded STEM experiences supported by mentorship, representation, and community connection. Its recent integration of artificial intelligence (AI) literacy reflects a growing recognition that early engagement with emerging technologies may expand access to future STEM learning opportunities. The paper discusses how AI-focused activities were introduced within this outreach model and examines short-term outcomes related to AI knowledge, confidence, and critical awareness. ### [201] [Reimagining Assessment in the Age of Generative AI: Lessons from Open-Book Exams with ChatGPT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12363)
*Qusay H. Mahmoud*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究通过让学生在开卷考试中使用ChatGPT并提交交互记录，发现学生与AI的互动呈现三种模式：答案检索、引导式协作和批判性验证。AI改变了评估的认知任务——从生成答案转向评估答案有效性，提示未来评估应关注学生对解决方案的推理能力而非独立产出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统学术评估假设学生独立完成工作，而生成式AI（如ChatGPT）挑战了这一假设。与其限制AI使用，不如探究学生如何在正式评估中实际与AI交互，以获取直接的推理过程证据（而非自我报告行为）。

Method: 工程专业学生在开卷带回家的考试中被允许使用ChatGPT，并被要求提交交互记录。通过对这些记录进行定性分析，识别学生使用AI的模式。

Result: 发现三种渐进式使用模式：答案检索（直接复制问题）、引导式协作（迭代优化提示）、批判性验证（评估AI的错误或不完整输出）。学生在调试、比较和验证AI输出时表现出最强的推理证据。

Conclusion: AI将评估的认知任务从产生解决方案转向评估解决方案的有效性。最终答案的正确性不再足以证明理解；提示编写、验证和判断等能力成为可见的学习指标。评估应发展成评估关于解决方案的推理，而非独立的解决方案产出。

Abstract: Generative AI systems such as ChatGPT challenge traditional assumptions about academic assessment by enabling students to generate explanations, code, and solutions in real time. Rather than attempting to restrict AI use, this study investigates how students actually interact with such systems during formal evaluation. Engineering students were permitted to use ChatGPT during take-home open-book exams and were required to submit interaction transcripts alongside exam solutions. This provided direct observational evidence of reasoning processes rather than relying on self-reported behavior. Qualitative analysis revealed three progressive patterns of use: answer retrieval, guided collaboration, and critical verification. While some students initially copied questions verbatim and received generic responses, many refined prompts iteratively and tested outputs. Some of the strongest evidence of reasoning appeared when students evaluated incorrect or incomplete AI responses, revealing evaluative reasoning through debugging, comparison, and justification. The presence of generative AI shifted the cognitive task of assessment from producing solutions to assessing solution validity. The findings suggest that, in AI-mediated assessment environments, correctness of final answers alone may no longer provide sufficient evidence of comprehension. Instead, competencies such as prompt formulation, verification, and judgment become visible indicators of learning. Transparent integration of AI appeared to reduce focus on rule avoidance and promote self-regulation. Assessments should evolve to evaluate reasoning about solutions rather than independent solution production. Generative AI therefore does not invalidate assessment but has the potential to expose deeper forms of understanding aligned with professional practice.

</details>

### [202] [A deep learning approach for pricing convertible bonds with path-dependent reset and call provisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12189)
*Qinwen Zhu,Wen Chen,Nicolas Langrené*

Main category: q-fin.PR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于深度学习框架的可转债定价方法，能够处理下行转股价重置和发行人赎回条款等路径依赖特征，在中国中信银行可转债上的实证显示方法稳定准确，并揭示了三个关键经济洞见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可转债市场广泛存在下行转股价重置和滚动窗口触发赎回等路径依赖条款，传统定价方法难以处理这些复杂特征，亟需一种高效灵活的定价工具。

Method: 将定价问题建模为路径依赖偏微分方程（PPDE），涵盖GBM、CEV、Heston三种基础资产动力学；构建离散时间动态规划方案，用神经网络近似条件期望，实现高维路径依赖场景下的可解性。

Result: 在中国中信银行可转债上的实证表明，该框架在所有模型设定下均生成稳定准确的价格和敏感性模式。

Conclusion: 1）合约条款对可转债价值的影响大于基础资产动力学；2）赎回条款通过截断上行收益降低价格；3）下行重置条款虽改善转换条件，但因降低有效赎回门槛、使提前赎回更可能，反而进一步降低价格。PPDE-深度学习方法为含复杂路径依赖结构的可转债定价提供了高效灵活的工具。

Abstract: This paper develops a deep learning-based framework for pricing convertible bonds with path-dependent contractual features, namely downward conversion price reset and issuer call clauses under rolling-window trigger rules, which are widespread in the convertible bond market. We formulate the valuation problem as a path-dependent partial differential equation (PPDE), which explicitly captures the dependence of the convertible bond value on the historical path of the underlying asset and the dynamic evolution of the conversion price. We derive consistent PPDE formulations for three canonical underlying dynamics: geometric Brownian motion (GBM), constant elasticity of variance (CEV) and Heston stochastic volatility. We then construct a discrete-time dynamic programming scheme in which conditional expectations are approximated by neural networks, which remains tractable in such high-dimensional path-dependent setting. Empirical tests on China CITIC Bank Convertible Bond show that our framework produces stable and accurate prices and sensitivity patterns across all model specifications. Three key economic insights emerge: 1. Contractual features dominate underlying dynamics in determining convertible bond values. 2. The call provision decreases convertible bonds prices by truncating upside gains. 3. Counterintuitively, despite improving conversion terms, the downward reset provision further decreases the price of convertible bonds by lowering the effective call threshold and making early redemption more likely. The proposed PPDE-deep learning approach provides an efficient, flexible tool for pricing convertible bonds with complex path-dependent structures.

</details>

### [203] [A Grid-Rate Condition for Valid Uniform Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12284)
*Emmanuel Selorm Tsyawo*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文研究了连续泛函估计中节点数 $L_n$ 的选择问题，证明了对于Donsker类中的函数，当 $L_n=ω(r_n^{1/4})$ 时能够保证渐近有效的推断，弥补了现有启发式方法缺乏形式化依据的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有连续泛函估计中节点数 $L_n$ 的选择缺乏严格的统计理论基础——固定$L$的经验法则和启发式数据驱动方法虽被广泛使用，但缺乏形式化依据。

Method: 利用实证过程理论，在Donsker类函数框架下，推导出节点增长条件 $L_n=ω(r_n^{1/4})$ 的理论充分性，确保近似误差相较于随机波动可渐近忽略。

Result: 证明了对于Donsker类中的函数，$L_n=ω(r_n^{1/4})$ 这一简单条件足以保证两次连续可微函数（以 $r_n^{1/2}$ 速率可估）的推断有效性。

Conclusion: 该条件为节点选择提供了理论保障，填补了现有方法缺乏形式化依据的空白，为实践中节点数的选择提供了可操作的指导。

Abstract: Estimating a continuous functional $F: \X \to \R$ involves specifying $L_n^d$ nodes on $\X \subset \R^d$ for estimation and uniform inference. While asymptotically valid inference requires $L_n$ to increase with $n$, existing fixed-$L$ rules of thumb and heuristic data-driven approaches lack formal justification. This paper shows that, for functions within a Donsker class, the simple grid-growth condition \(L_n=ω(r_n^{1/4})\) is sufficient for valid inference for twice continuously differentiable functions estimable at the \(r_n^{1/2}\) rate. This condition ensures that the approximation error is asymptotically negligible relative to the stochastic variation of the empirical process.

### [204] [The Value of Information: A Puzzle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11180)
*Ohad Kadan,Asaf Manela*

Main category: q-fin.GN

TL;DR: 本文发现，在温和假设下，信息对知情交易者的总价值可通过价格变动与订单流的协方差衡量，该协方差等于噪声交易者的损失。基于美国股票高频数据估算，平均每年每只股票的信息价值约350万美元，总信息价值约占市值的0.04%，远低于投资者每年为寻求超额回报支付的0.67%费用（French, 2008）。文章探讨了这一令人困惑的发现背后的可能解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者希望量化金融市场中信息对知情交易者的实际价值，并解释为何信息价值远低于投资者为获取信息优势所支付的成本（如管理费、研究费用等），从而揭示金融市场信息效率与投资者实际支出之间的巨大落差。

Method: 理论上，作者证明在市场竞争性做市的条件下，知情交易者的信息价值等于噪声交易者的损失，即价格变动与订单流的协方差。实证上，作者使用美国股票的高频交易数据，通过估计价格变化与订单流的协方差来计算信息价值。

Result: 平均每只股票每年的信息价值约为350万美元。市场总信息价值约占市值的0.04%，远低于French（2008）估算的投资者每年为寻找超额收益所支付的0.67%费用。

Conclusion: 信息价值远低于投资者为获取信息优势所支付的成本，存在明显的"信息价值悖论"。作者呼吁进一步研究这一差距的成因，可能包括投资者过度自信、非理性行为、代理问题或信息的外部性等。

Abstract: We show that under mild assumptions, the total value of information to informed traders in the market can be measured by the covariance between price changes and order flow. This covariance captures noise trader losses, which equal informed trader gains when market making is competitive. We estimate the value of information using high frequency data on US equities at about $3.5 million per year for the average stock. The aggregate value of information is about 0.04% of market cap, which is considerably lower than the 0.67% in fees investors pay each year searching for superior returns (French 2008). We discuss potential resolutions for these puzzling findings.

</details>

### [205] [Optimal Control of the Ethena Yield-Bearing Stablecoin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11263)
*Matthew Lorig*

Main category: q-fin.MF

TL;DR: 本文通过随机控制模型分析了Ethena协议的核心收益策略——同时做多stETH和做空ETH永续合约构成Delta中性组合，并考虑了永久性和暂时性两类价格冲击，分别给出了无限期折现和有限期两种情形下的最优控制显式解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为去中心化金融（DeFi）领域的稳定币协议Ethena的收益生成策略提供严格的数学建模和最优控制理论支撑，理解价格冲击对策略收益的影响机制。

Method: 建立随机控制问题，模型包含两种价格冲击（永久性冲击改变市场中间价、压缩基差，暂时性冲击反映执行滑点），分别求解无限期折现问题和有限期最大化总财富问题，得到最优控制的显式解。

Result: 在无限期折现和有限期两种设定下，均得到了最优控制策略的显式表达式。

Conclusion: 论文为Ethena协议的Delta中性收益策略提供了量化最优控制框架，明确指出在执行过程中需权衡永久性价格冲击（侵蚀未来收益）与暂时性冲击（执行成本）。

Abstract: We formulate and solve stochastic control problems that model the core yield-generating strategy of the Ethena protocol, a decentralized finance (DeFi) stablecoin that earns yield by combining a long position in staked Ethereum (stETH) with an equal-sized short position in ETH perpetual futures. The combined position is delta-neutral with respect to the ETH spot price, yet earns carry from two sources: staking rewards on the stETH leg, and funding-rate payments received from long perpetual holders when the perpetual trades at a premium to spot. A key feature of our model is that the control -- the rate of simultaneously buying stETH and shorting the perpetual -- exerts two distinct types of price impact. \textit{Permanent} impact shifts the mid-market prices of both legs, compressing the basis and permanently eroding future funding income. \textit{Temporary} impact reflects execution slippage on each leg. We study both an infinite-horizon discounted problem and a finite-horizon problem in which the protocol maximizes total wealth up to a fixed date $T$, subject to a terminal cost for liquidating any remaining position. In both cases the optimal control is obtained explicitly.

</details>


### [206] [On convergence of the Mayer problems arising in the theory of financial markets with transaction cost](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11717)
*Yuri Kabanov,Artur Sidorenko*

Main category: q-fin.MF

TL;DR: 本文在含比例交易成本的金融市场几何框架下，研究了随机Mayer控制问题（最大化终端财富期望效用），并得到了价格近似下最优值与最优控制的连续性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将含比例交易成本的金融市场（股票、货币等）从参数化具体模型嵌入到由过程S（价格）和K（偿付集）定义的随机框架中，该框架允许利用集值技术研究无套利、对冲、组合优化等基本问题。本文希望在此一般框架下进一步探索随机Mayer控制问题。

Method: 在几何形式主义描述的多资产一般框架下，将随机Mayer控制问题（最大化组合终端财富的期望效用）形式化，通过价格近似分析研究最优值与最优控制的连续性。

Result: 在价格近似下，得到了最优值的连续性和最优控制的连续性结果。

Conclusion: 本文在含比例交易成本的金融市场几何框架下，成功将随机Mayer控制问题纳入该一般框架，并证明了价格近似下最优值与最优控制的连续性，为后续集值技术应用提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The geometric approach to financial markets with proportional transaction cost prescribes to imbed a specific model (of stock market, of currency market etc.), usually given in a parametric form, into a natural framework defined by the two random processes, S and K. The first one, d-dimensional, models the price evolution of basic securities while the second one, cone-valued, describes the evolution of the solvency set. It happened that the fundamental questions -- no-arbitrage criteria, hedging problems, portfolio optimization -- can be studied in this general setting opening the door to set-valued techniques. In this note we explore, in such a general framework, the stochastic Mayer control problem, consisting in the maximization of the expected utility of the portfolio terminal wealth. We get results on continuity of the optimal value and the optimal control under price approximations in a general multi-asset framework described by the geometric formalism.

</details>
